Current Commentary

Parent-Teacher Associations and the Issue of Maternal Education 18

— Duan

The National Children's Year Implementation Committee has recently promulgated the organizational outline for parent-teacher associations. The objectives of parent-teacher associations are: 1. To cultivate the intelligence and virtue of parents. 2. To research and implement child-rearing methods. 3. To promote the happiness of children. Currently, our country's society is becoming increasingly corrupt, and the people's self-confidence has disappeared. Carelessness, laziness, opportunism, and taking shortcuts have become common practices. If we improve from the family aspect and seek to correct past bad habits, enabling parents to have the intelligence to raise modern children, it is an urgent task today. This is why parent-teacher associations are being promoted. However, the Chinese people lack experience in gatherings. This is true in cities, and even more so in rural areas. Now, to accomplish this goal, we must put more effort into publicity, guidance, and demonstration.

Throughout history, historians have invariably attributed the achievements of successful individuals to their maternal education, while rarely mentioning paternal education. This does not mean that fathers do not teach, but rather that the reasons why paternal education does not match maternal education have already been stated by Mencius. Gongsun Chou asked Mencius, "Why is it that a gentleman does not teach his own son?" Mencius said, "It is impossible to impose it. To teach a son, one must do so with righteousness. If righteousness is not followed, one continues with anger. If one continues with anger, the relationship is ruined. If you, as a father, teach me with righteousness, but you yourself do not act righteously, then the father and son will harm each other. If the father and son harm each other, then it is bad." Therefore, ancient people exchanged children for education. The father's education was entrusted to the teacher, while the family relied on maternal education as its foundation. Mothers are inherently kind and spend a lot of time with their children, so their teachings are easily accepted. This is why wise mothers have wise children, and wise children often credit their wise mothers. Now, everything can be equal between men and women, except for the duties of inherent roles. We cannot force them to be the same, nor can we abandon them. This is not only a personal problem, but also related to the survival of the nation.

However, today's so-called ladies often rely on the economic support of men and forget their responsibilities. They indulge in ease and enjoyment, holding a mahjong tile in hand, neglecting everything. They view housework as a lowly task, entrusting childcare to servants, and even think that this is necessary to be considered liberated. Is this not a great delusion? Paternal education is declining, and maternal education is deteriorating. Children are influenced by what they hear and see, and habits become second nature. Who can take responsibility for nurturing righteousness? Even if there is excellent school education, it is no different from one day of sunshine followed by ten days of cold. What good does it do? Therefore, the most important issue in saving the country is still how to cultivate good citizens. But to have good citizens, we must have good parents, especially virtuous maternal education.

Speech by Representative Yan at the League of Nations Assembly: China is Willing to Contribute to World Peace; World Politicians Emphasize European Security; The League of Nations Lacks Courage to Guide Breakers of Agreements to the Law 19

(Geneva) Our representative, Ambassador Yan Huiqing, gave a speech at the League of Nations Assembly this morning, stating briefly that the countries that are the mainstay of the League of Nations, at this time when the situation in Europe is precarious and unstable, should be clearly aware that world peace depends on their efforts, so as to give the League of Nations new life. This is something the Chinese government is deeply gratified by. If the League of Nations fails to exercise its authority again this time, then this cornerstone of maintaining international peace will inevitably collapse completely. Therefore, the major powers who are willing to take responsibility loudly proclaim that their foreign policy must be based on the League of Nations, and local matters should also be subject to agreements to ensure security and supplement what the covenant has not covered. For a year, European politicians have been working hard and anxiously to maintain peace in Europe and even the world. Geneva, Rome, London, Stresa, and Moscow have all been major achievements in this effort. The term "collective security" is almost known to every household. The correct interpretation of collective security should be that every member state of the League of Nations should be protected from aggression by the collective actions of other member states. The League of Nations Covenant not only protects a member state from aggression by other member states, but also protects it from aggression by non-member states. The key to collective security lies in the League of Nations, and once a country joins as a member, it is as if it has assumed the responsibility of jointly safeguarding its territorial and political sovereignty. If all member states can consistently fulfill their obligations in accordance with their covenant, then why does collective security need new treaties or new procedures to be obtained? For obvious reasons, the League of Nations has failed to maintain universal collective security? As a result, countries around the world, especially in Europe, are building local collective security arrangements as alternatives. Such local agreements, if not contrary to the spirit of the covenant, are not to be criticized. However, because universal collective security has not been obtained, and it is necessary to seek second best, the situation is also quite sad. It should be known that the collective security contained in the League of Nations Covenant is pure and cannot be analyzed. Its simplicity and inseparability from world peace is the same as the security of European countries, which is the security of other countries in the world, and it cannot be said that the security of one place is more important than the security of another place, nor can it be said that the security of one country is more important than the security of another country. Now the world organization, with economic and other relations becoming increasingly close, the impact of one part of the world reaches other parts in an instant. Damage to the security of one country affects the entire world. In recent years, world politicians have often paid close attention to European politics, while events in other places are considered insignificant. Even if there are disagreements in principle or violations of the covenant, they are willing to compromise in order to maintain temporary peace, not knowing that this kind of peace is just a false name, and the actual harm will be seen in the long run, and future conflicts will be rooted in this. The reason why the League of Nations is the League of Nations lies in its internationality and universality. The past failures of the League of Nations are not because it has no means, but because it has no courage to guide violators of agreements to the law. This is also why China and other countries are disappointed. The Chinese people love peace and sincerely support the principles contained in the Covenant. Their faith in the League of Nations has not only not diminished, but now that China is the only member of the League of Nations in the Far East, it is enough to strengthen its great desire to contribute to world peace, cooperation, and security, hoping only to obtain an opportunity to realize its ambitions. (Central News Agency dispatch, 11th)

Turning Point in the History of the League of Nations: British Foreign Secretary Hoare's Declaration; Deep Impression in Europe; Stimulating Joint Action by France; Italy Waits for Laval to Express Himself Today 20

(Rome) Italy believes that tomorrow will be one of the most important days in the history of the League of Nations, because French Prime Minister Laval will decide whether France will obey British proposals or join forces with its Latin sister countries. Everyone acknowledges that there is an unbridgeable gap between the positions of Britain and Italy. Britain feels that the way for the League of Nations to survive is to seek peaceful solutions, and there is no other way. Italy, on the other hand, believes that the Abyssinian issue has nothing to do with the League of Nations, and letting Italy and Abyssinia resolve it themselves is the only way for the League of Nations to survive. With such different views, it is almost impossible to reconcile them. It is rumored that if French Prime Minister Laval's remarks do not satisfy the Italians, Italy will withdraw from the League of Nations, but it will not do so unless absolutely necessary. This is Italy's current attitude. (Reuters dispatch, 12th)

(Geneva) From the Italian side, it is rumored that French Prime Minister Laval will submit several proposals to the Committee of Five of the League of Nations Council today. If accepted by the committee, they will be sent to Italian Representative Aloisi. It is said that Aloisi has agreed to consider them carefully. Many feel that British Foreign Secretary Hoare's remarks should not be overemphasized, as British cabinet members have already made similar remarks elsewhere. This is just a restatement of previous events, but the tone is slightly more severe than before. (Reuters dispatch, 12th)

(London) British Foreign Secretary Hoare's remarks at the League of Nations Assembly yesterday, explaining Britain's attitude towards the Italian-Abyssinian dispute, have made a deep impression on European countries. People in Paris consider the remarks of the British Foreign Secretary to be a turning point in the history of the League of Nations. People in Geneva see this as a warning to France and the League of Nations, implying "Move forward, or we will withdraw." People in Rome also consider this a warning to France, meaning that if the League of Nations cannot peacefully resolve the Abyssinian issue, Britain will no longer be involved in European affairs in the future. The Italian writer Gayda published an article in the Italian Daily, saying that the British government wants to impose difficult problems on France. Without joint action against Italy, there will be Britain's departure from European affairs. Of the two, choosing one, for France's sake, the assistance of a strongly united Italy is more valuable than the twists and turns of British policy. Italians unanimously believe that Mussolini will not change his policy slightly because of the British Foreign Secretary's remarks. The British Foreign Secretary's remarks only make Italy more likely to withdraw from the League of Nations. Political circles in Rome claim that Italian Representative Aloisi will not respond to the remarks of Hoare or Laval when he speaks, because Rome believes that the Abyssinian issue, as far as Geneva is concerned, has now ended. It is said that Hoare had previously shown his speech draft to Laval, and Laval decided to postpone his response until Friday, apparently wanting to consult with his colleagues before giving a substantive answer. Laval hopes that Italy may slightly narrow the scope after hearing the British Foreign Secretary's remarks, but observers feel that this may not be possible. To what extent will France prepare to back Britain in upholding the League of Nations Covenant? It will be seen in the French Prime Minister's speech. In addition to Hoare's remarks and the demand for changing the status quo supported by national prestige, and the right of backward countries to maintain their independence, what France pays the most attention to is Hoare's proposal for a global investigation to correct the inappropriate distribution of profit sources. Germany also paid great attention to Hoare's remarks. The Berlin Daily said that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini's wording was strong, and the British remarks were also equally strong, tit-for-tat, which is unprecedented in the history of the League of Nations. Although the wording is still mild, the rift between Britain and Italy is deepening, and even the most optimistic cannot hold optimistic illusions. According to the newspaper's opinion, Hoare's remarks can only make Italy's already adopted attitude stronger. (Reuters dispatch, 12th)

British and French Representatives Talk; Hoare Postpones Return to Country 21

(London) According to responsible sources, British Foreign Secretary Hoare's speech at the League of Nations Assembly yesterday is now a question being explored by France. It is said that the French ambassador has inquired with the British Foreign Office whether the British Foreign Secretary's speech contains the meaning that Britain currently firmly upholds the attitude of the League of Nations Covenant, and will take this attitude in the future when there are cases of aggression in Europe, especially aggression against Austria. (Reuters dispatch, 12th)

(Geneva) French Prime Minister Laval, British Foreign Secretary Hoare, and Minister Without Portfolio Eden held talks this evening. According to information obtained by our special correspondent, these talks were not limited to the Abyssinian issue, but also discussed the implementation of a European collective security system. In other words, the important points included in the Anglo-French London Declaration of February 3 this year, such as the conclusion of the Sky Locarno Treaty, the Danube Treaty, and the Eastern European Treaty, were discussed. As for the British Foreign Secretary Hoare's speech at the League of Nations Assembly, people in political circles here feel the greatest impression after learning about it, believing that it is the first time that the British representative has explained the country's obligations on the European continent in such a clear tone. It is generally expected that French Prime Minister Laval will submit a request to the Council's Committee on the Italian-Abyssinian Dispute tomorrow, asking it to continue its efforts to find a peaceful solution. Therefore, the committee seems to be preparing a report on the circumstances of the dispute and formulating appropriate proposals for resolving the dispute, which will be submitted to the Council and then adopted by the Council. (Havas dispatch, 11th)

(Geneva) French Prime Minister Laval recently invited British Foreign Secretary Hoare and Minister Without Portfolio Eden to lunch in Geneva for talks. Foreign Secretary Hoare was originally scheduled to return to Britain tomorrow morning, but because he wanted to hear Laval's speech on the Italian-Abyssinian dispute, he has postponed his departure until tomorrow afternoon. (Havas dispatch, 12th)

(Geneva) British Foreign Secretary Hoare, who was scheduled to return to Britain today, has now decided to postpone his departure until tomorrow. French Foreign Minister Laval was supposed to give a speech to the League of Nations Assembly today, but after full consideration with Hoare and Eden, he also decided to postpone his speech until tomorrow. According to the French delegation, the scope of the talks between the two cabinet members is not limited to the Abyssinian issue, but also includes all the issues in the Anglo-French rescue declaration of February 3. (National Telegram, 12th)

(Geneva) French Representative, Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval is scheduled to deliver a speech at the League of Nations Assembly tomorrow. It is said that the main points of his speech are necessary for safeguarding the principles of the League of Nations Covenant, and are consistent with the British Foreign Secretary Hoare's speech this morning. However, in order to avoid causing war, Laval advocates that the Italian-Abyssinian issue should continue to be reconciled until the dispute is resolved. Laval insists that the Five-Power Committee should draft a proposal to resolve the Italian-Abyssinian dispute. If this proposal is approved by the League of Nations Council, it can be submitted to both Italy and Abyssinia. If this procedure is adopted, then in the event of reconciliation failure, who should be responsible for its failure will be clear at a glance. (Havas dispatch, 11th)

(Geneva) Britain demands that the League of Nations oppose Italy's militarism with all its strength. France's position has become more important because Prime Minister Laval's last request for compromise from Mussolini over the phone was unsuccessful. It is said that after Laval's proposal was rejected by Italy, France will become more inclined to Britain, appease the League of Nations, and test whether Italy can destroy the League of Nations Covenant. Most of the representatives of all countries in the League of Nations Assembly also expressed their intention to support Britain in deciding whether the League of Nations will remain without integrity and be ridiculed by the world, or will stake everything with all its strength to prevent Mussolini. (National Telegram, 11th)

(London) Political circles in London welcome British Foreign Secretary Hoare's remarks at the League of Nations Assembly yesterday, because they clarify Britain's position more clearly than before. Political circles in London are now awaiting the French government's expression. It is said that in diplomatic circles, France's attitude has recently tended to favor collective action. It is expected that the League of Nations Economic Committee will be asked to study the entire issue of managing raw material supply. All sectors in Britain unanimously support Hoare's remarks, saying that his meaning is clear and leaves no room for misunderstanding. The Times called this an authoritative and historically valuable declaration that is related to British policy. The League of Nations must show that there are other ways to achieve legitimate national goals besides war. The Daily Telegraph reported that if other countries are unwilling to implement the resolutions of the League of Nations, Britain will slacken its support for collective security. The Morning Post reported that Hoare's remarks did not include the suggestion that Britain would act alone in the worst case. Other newspapers criticized this similarly, but a few Labor Party newspapers, such as the Daily Mail, said that Hoare's remarks increased the fear that Britain would be drawn into a European war. (Reuters dispatch, 12th)

(London) In his speech at the League of Nations Assembly yesterday, British Foreign Secretary Hoare concluded by saying, "This is the attitude that Britain holds towards the League of Nations Covenant. If the League of Nations is still an effective mechanism, and Britain's connection with the European continent remains intact, then I do not believe that this attitude will change." Reuters has learned that it would be inappropriate to interpret Hoare's words as meaning that if the League of Nations is ineffective, Britain will withdraw from the organization. His words expressed that if the League of Nations cannot be an effective mechanism in the Italian-Abyssinian dispute, then Britain and other countries in the League of Nations will reconsider their membership in the League of Nations. (Reuters dispatch, 12th)

(Paris) The Paris Evening News's special correspondent in Geneva declared that British Foreign Secretary Hoare believed that Italy would start fighting Abyssinia in early October, so he asked France to join Britain in putting pressure on Italy, and proposed that the Council's Committee on the Italian-Abyssinian Dispute draft a final proposal, and let Italy reject it and bear the responsibility. When the time comes, if Italy rejects the proposal and starts firing, then the League of Nations should decide on appropriate measures, but not in the form of sanctions, and its nature should be economic rather than military. (Havas dispatch, 12th)

(Geneva) According to reports, French Prime Minister Laval rejected the proposal to take sanctions, which was quite surprising to those who heard about it in the League of Nations lounge. The French delegation recently declared that the French government's attitude towards the Italian-Abyssinian dispute will be explained by Prime Minister Laval in a speech tomorrow morning. As for the news circulating outside, which is not without contradictions, it is not formal or semi-official. (Havas dispatch, 12th)

Laval and Mussolini; Telephone Contact Fails; Committee to Submit Report 22

(Geneva) The League of Nations Five-Power Committee is scheduled to hold an important meeting this afternoon. At that time, French Prime Minister Laval will announce the results of the negotiations. Laval tried to contact Mussolini by phone yesterday but failed, and plans to try again today. If there is no possibility of compromise with Italy, then the Five-Power Committee will only be able to submit a report to the League of Nations Council. What has not been decided is whether this report should be submitted to Italy and Abyssinia first, or directly to the League of Nations Council. According to information from the British delegation, Britain will not let the League of Nations Council adjourn until the final solution is decided. Even if Italy rejects all proposals and the League of Nations Council passes a final report against Italy, the League of Nations Council will meet until October, waiting for Italy's actions in East Africa, and then act according to the situation. (National Telegram, 12th)

Britain Holds Important Cabinet Meeting; Both Naval and Army Authorities Attend 23

(London) An important cabinet meeting was held at 10 Downing Street today, chaired by Prime Minister Baldwin. Participants included Lord President of the Council MacDonald, First Lord of the Admiralty Monsell, Air Secretary Lister, War Secretary Halifax, Colonial Secretary Malcolm MacDonald, Permanent Under-Secretary of the Foreign Office Vansittart, and technical advisors on army, navy, and air force defense. The meeting lasted for two hours, and its nature is not yet known, but it is said that there is no special relationship. According to ordinary observers, the attendance of the Colonial Secretary and the Secretaries of the Army, Navy, and Air Force is particularly noteworthy. (Reuters dispatch, 11th)

(London) The British Army declared today that the War Office, in view of the international situation, has decided to restore the number of troops stationed in Malta to its pre-1929 level, because in 1929, the troops stationed in Malta were transferred to Palestine, and the quota has not been replenished since then. Therefore, two infantry battalions currently stationed in Catterick, England, will be sent to Malta. (Reuters dispatch, 12th)

(Cairo) There are currently more than 300 British aircraft in Egypt. Two aircraft carriers are docked in Alexandria, each carrying five squadrons of air force. There are 120 aircraft in Abu Qir to defend the Suez Canal. (National Telegram, 12th)

Italian Army Accelerates Departure to East Africa; Purchases of Rubber Triple 24

(Rome) The Italian army's departure to East Africa is increasing. Three ships in the port of Naples, carrying 6,000 soldiers, are firing up their engines and waiting to depart. Another 3,600 soldiers are sailing from Genoa. From Venice, 100 artisans are also sailing to East Africa. (National Telegram, 12th)

(Colombo) According to figures released by customs today, Italy's purchase of Ceylon rubber in August was almost three times that of July. (Reuters dispatch, 12th)

(Rome) Since war between Italy and Abyssinia is inevitable, according to observations in Roman diplomatic circles, the war will begin around October 10. (Japan Dispatch, 12th)

Representatives of Belgium, Sweden, and the Netherlands; Support League of Nations Covenant; Willing to Fulfill All Obligations 25

(Geneva) Belgian Prime Minister Janson stated at the League of Nations Assembly this morning the attitude of Belgium towards the League of Nations Covenant, saying that Belgium is determined to actively proceed to fulfill its obligations under the League of Nations Covenant, and is willing to assume joint responsibility. The Foreign Ministers of Sweden and the Netherlands also spoke, declaring their willingness to continue to uphold the League of Nations and fulfill their covenant obligations. Belgian Prime Minister Janson spoke first, followed by Swedish Prime Minister Sandler, saying that the remarks issued by Italy on January 19, stating that the nature of the Walwal border incident would not harm the peaceful relations between Italy and Abyssinia, are inconsistent with the current situation. Italy's memorandum to the League of Nations did not indicate that Abyssinia's actions had fundamentally changed Italy's claims. The Swedish government wants the League of Nations to fulfill its responsibilities and investigate Italy's accusations of Abyssinian slavery. Dutch Foreign Minister Graeff spoke last, saying that a small country that has maintained neutrality for more than a century has abandoned its neutrality when it joined the League of Nations, and to uphold the implementation of the principles of the League of Nations, the League of Nations should fulfill its responsibilities. One of the difficulties is the inequality in the distribution of raw materials, and the obstacles to world trade caused by tariff barriers and currency restrictions. He believes that the full implementation of the open-door policy should be the key to the world system. The Netherlands is loyal to the League of Nations and is willing to fulfill all its obligations. (Reuters dispatch, 12th)

Germany to Announce Policy; Hitler to Convene Reichstag on the 15th 26

(London) According to information released by responsible sources, German leader Hitler plans to convene the Reichstag in Nuremberg on the 15th, hoping to deliver an important speech on German foreign policy. (Havas dispatch, 12th)

(Berlin) It is said that Hitler will convene a temporary meeting of the Reichstag in Nuremberg on the afternoon of September 15. The reason for its convocation is still a mystery. According to propaganda officials, they know nothing about this. It is believed that Hitler may want to issue a foreign policy declaration on the Italian-Abyssinian dispute, or want to ask the Reichstag to pass measures to deal with the Jewish issue and church affairs.

Abyssinian Representative Speaks; Welcomes Economic Development; Asks League of Nations to Send Personnel to Investigate the Truth 27

(Geneva) Abyssinian Representative to the League of Nations Assembly, Halewillet, today requested the assembly to send personnel to Abyssinia to investigate whether Abyssinia is a barbaric country as Italy claims. Halewillet also said that if there is evidence of barbarism, with the precision of modern photography, it would not be difficult to reveal it completely. Halewillet also said that Abyssinia is ready to welcome international assistance to develop its resources, and is prepared to accept any reasonable suggestions that come from sincerity. Although Abyssinia is accused of being a barbaric country, it has proven its ability to restrain and be humble in this crisis. As for the condemnation of the slave system, it did not originate in Abyssinia. Even the lives of workers in factories in some civilized countries may not be much higher than those of slaves. (National Telegram, 11th)

(Geneva) Abyssinia's chief representative, Halewillet, gave a very mild speech at the League of Nations Assembly. Halewillet was short in stature, standing in front of the table, barely taller than the table. Halewillet said, "We welcome impartial steps from the League of Nations to improve Abyssinia's economic level. We should see these steps as a friendly gesture to guide us onto the path of progress." Halewillet then cited President Wilson's principle of "self-determination is best," and said that he believed that the League of Nations had ended the era of conquest by force and guaranteed the freedom of all mankind. Australian Representative Bruce said that he did not want to hinder the dispute with dangerous words, but only wanted to ask whether any action taken in Geneva would not be protected by instruments such as the League of Nations Covenant, the Kellogg-Briand Pact, the Locarno Treaty, and the Stresa Agreement. If the current difficulties faced by the League of Nations cannot be resolved, can these things survive? Next, the Hungarian representative spoke, urging Hungary to be granted equal armament rights. The last speaker was the Norwegian representative, saying that Norway had previously opposed Abyssinia's accession to the League of Nations due to the evolution of Abyssinia's social conditions, but the League of Nations should now treat both parties fairly and strive to prevent the two countries from fighting each other.

The assembly adjourned at 7:15 p.m. until 10:00 a.m. tomorrow, thus ending one of the most tense days Geneva has seen in many years. After the adjournment, British Foreign Secretary Hoare. Minister Without Portfolio The Abyssinian issue has lasted for a long time, and they also explored the overall situation in Europe based on the Anglo-French agreement of February 3. After the discussion, the Five-Person Special Committee continued to study Italy's memorandum stating that Abyssinia was not qualified to be a member of the League of Nations. Eden and Laval were both members of the committee, so they also attended the meeting. (Reuters dispatch, 11th)

Italy Also Courts France; Hoping to Localize East African War 28

(Rome) Mussolini's confidant, the famous reporter Gayda, recently published an article in the "Italian Daily" to comment on Britain's attitude towards the Italian-Abyssinian dispute, saying that when China and Japan had a dispute over the Northeast China issue, Britain did not ask the League of Nations to impose sanctions on Japan. Now, towards Italy, it has changed its past attitude and firmly advocated it. "As for France, Laval has not expressed his approval of the sanctions proposed by Britain, and therefore has not only not hindered the authority of the League of Nations, but has also preserved it. This is logical and consistent."

It also said that France's rejection of British proposals has various reasons. One is that the British House of Commons may be re-elected, and the Labor Party may win, then British foreign policy will change. This is not in France's interest. Italy, on the other hand, is deeply willing to maintain friendship with France and make the Italian-Abyssinian conflict a local conflict. In other words, it is to maintain the nature of this conflict as a colonial war. (Havas dispatch, 12th)

Italy Proposes Treaty with Germany; Saying it is Not Accurate to Conclude a Non-Aggression Treaty 29

(Rome) The semi-official Stefani News Agency recently officially denied rumors that the Italian government proposed to conclude a non-aggression treaty with Germany. (Havas dispatch, 11th)

League of Nations to Discuss Adding Chinese Council Seat Today 30

(Geneva) The League of Nations Administrative Council is scheduled to reconvene at 5 PM on Friday to decide whether the League of Nations General Assembly will add an administrative council seat for China. The League of Nations Administrative Council last added a non-permanent seat on October 9, 1933, for Portugal. China, after being elected on September 15, 1931, did not seek re-election after its three-year term expired, hence today's event. (National Telegram, 12th)

Hitler Sworn In: Germany Continues Military Expansion, Eliminates Internal Traitors, Advances Courageously, Guarantees to Avoid Inflation, Educates the People to Serve the Public 31

Nuremberg - After the Fuhrer Hitler's right-hand man, Hess, delivered the opening address, all 20,000 representatives in the audience stood up and cheered. Schwede then delivered a brief speech to welcome the conference representatives. Chancellor Hitler thanked him and shook his hand warmly. Then, local leader Wagner read Hitler's declaration, first outlining the remarkable achievements of the National Socialist Party, especially noting that the number of unemployed people in Germany had decreased from six million to one million seven hundred and fifty thousand.

He also stated that Germany had gained military autonomy since the promulgation of the conscription system, and then compared Germany's security with the insecurity abroad, saying that Germany was no longer a plaything without the ability to defend itself, but its protection was not based on treaties, but on the nation's determination and strength. If it were a weak country today, disaster would surely befall it. The so-called justice of the world is merely an illusion. Even more, the resources of these weak countries are considered to be under the control of strong countries. Adherents of pacifism are actually engaging in the manufacture of war, but Germany aims to live in harmony with its neighbors.

Hitler's declaration then touched on the internal traitors of the National Socialist government, divided into three categories: (1) Jewish Marxism and parliamentary democracy; (2) the Catholic Center Party, which politically and morally poisoned the people; (3) the incorrigible middle-class reactionaries. These three types of internal traitors initially thought that the revolution of 1933 meant nothing more than a change of government, and hoped that the government would still change after three years. But as of today, the National Socialist government is moving forward and becoming more stable, which has greatly alarmed them. Unstable elements in the financial world have changed their reserved attitude and turned to waving flags and shouting, hoping to hinder the progress of the National Socialist Party, but they will eventually suffer the consequences. To the followers of Marxism and the Jews, we have only one word: we have given them a way to rehabilitate themselves. If they can live in peace, we may not remember old grievances, but we ultimately feel that this compassion is misunderstood, and the result will be inevitable. After eliminating this danger, the National Socialist Party will advance courageously. We are wrong to believe that the bureaucratization of the government is not suitable to solve certain problems, because we believe that the country will be humiliated by these problems. On the contrary, we should do our best to solve any problem that can be solved. Problems that the government cannot solve will be solved by the National Socialist movement. If necessary, the government will definitely pass laws to transfer institutions unsuitable to deal with them to agencies we deem suitable to solve these events.

Regarding the church issue, the declaration stated that the National Socialist Party never intended to resist Christianity, but could not tolerate the church engaging in political work. People need not doubt the government and the National Socialist Party's determination on this matter. The declaration also recounted the major events of the National Socialist Party and the government last year, as well as the economic situation, and firmly guaranteed to avoid inflation, so an increase in wages and prices is also impossible. The declaration finally revealed the major policies for the coming year as follows: (1) strive to alleviate unemployment; (2) maintain the current wages; (3) further strengthen military power, so as to be a pillar of European peace and culture; (4) continue to strive to produce raw materials, so that Germany is economically self-sufficient; (5) educate the people, so that they become a true national society, because it is necessary to eliminate many prejudices and evil forces, so it is the most difficult task. (National Telegram, 11th) Nuremberg, Hitler, in the afternoon, presided over the groundbreaking ceremony of the National Socialist Party Congress hall in front of 20,000 uniformed National Socialist Party members. The hall will take eight years to complete. The hall is so large that it can accommodate 60,000 people. Mr. Hitler gave a brief speech, saying that this is the first major project in the Third German State. When completed, representatives of the National Socialist Party will gather in this hall every year for countless centuries. After the ceremony, many rounds of field artillery were fired to celebrate.

The National Socialist Party Congress today read Hitler's declaration, which criticized President Wilson's famous Fourteen Points presented at the 1918 conference, and contained statements such as Germany no longer trusts the world, but will rely on its own strength to survive, Germany is no longer a football, no longer an object of foreign strategy, and Germany cannot tolerate any attempt to harm its power. (Reuters Telegram, 11th)

Nuremberg - Today is the second day of the National Socialist Party Congress. The work of the congress is completely focused on compulsory labor service. Since last year's congress, the development of labor service has been remarkable, and there is also female labor service for the first time. In the afternoon, Hitler and labor leader Heur will speak to the crowd. In the evening, there will be a grand torch parade. (National Telegram, 12th)

(Geneva) Our country's envoy to Turkey, He Yaotu, arrived here on the 9th and set off for Berlin today to attend the National Socialist Party Congress. Mr. He will return to Geneva within days to attend the League of Nations Congress. (Central News Agency Telegram, 12th)

British Economic Envoy Ross Meets Takahashi, Manchurian Tobacco Company Opposes British American Tobacco Company 32

(Tokyo) British government chief economic advisor Mr. Ross is scheduled to visit Finance Minister Takahashi at 2 PM on the 13th to discuss financial and fiscal issues in Japan and various issues related to Sino-Japanese relations. (Japan United News Telegram, 12th)

(Tokyo) The Manchurian Tobacco Company, which was not established last year, has a capital of 12 million Japanese yen and plans to sell its products by the end of March next year. If the accuser only requests the prosecutor of the second instance to file an appeal according to the appeal procedure according to Article 25, Paragraph 1 of the chapter, it is still different from the self-accusation of the plaintiff and should be handled according to the precedent according to Article 25, Paragraph 2 of the chapter, with the prosecutor as the appellant. Cotton and Wheat

US Cotton: The New York cotton market opened down 3 to 5 pounds. There was a large amount of hedging, causing the price to continue to fall 2 to 3 pounds at 11 AM. Although there were slight gains, they could not affect the market price. It only rose back by 2 pounds at 11:20 AM.

British Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market fell slightly today. The October futures price fell 1 pound to 5.77.

British Wheat: The Liverpool wheat market was firm this morning. At 1 PM, the October futures price was 6 shillings and 0.75 pence, up 0.25.

US Wheat: The Chicago wheat market opened up 0.625 due to strong overseas news. Market interest gradually increased, and the market price continued to rise 0.625. However, there was profit-taking later, causing the recent price to be 0.75 lower than the opening price. The opening price of miscellaneous grains rose 0.25 along with the wheat price, and then continued to rise and fall along with the wheat market. The recent price fell 0.25 lower than the opening price.

Rubber

New York: The London rubber market continued to be quiet. At noon, the January-March futures price was 5.625 pence, down 0.0625.

Public Telegram 64

To the Editors of the Shen Bao with Respectful Consideration,

We, Ying Shang, are innocent, yet we repeatedly encounter great disasters. Floods struck in the year of Xinwei, a severe epidemic raged in the year of Renshen, and now, in this year of Guiyou, bandits from Henan are rampaging throughout our territory. Within three years, the people and their possessions have been devastated, and their vitality has been depleted. Long ago, nine out of ten households were empty, and the people could barely survive. Unexpectedly, this year's wheat harvest was again poor, and now we are further afflicted by drought. From March until now, there have been only two instances of slight rainfall. The scorching heat is more intense than fire, and the fields are cracked open by several feet. The seedlings have withered and died almost completely, and the red earth stretches for thousands of miles. The hope of life is almost extinguished. Alas! While the river basins are suffering from excessive rain, our corner of Ying is suffering from such a severe drought. Why does Heaven not have pity and bring about something that should not exist, but does? Now that we have reached Mid-Autumn Festival, no food can be planted, and if it still does not rain, the rural areas will collapse, and the situation will become even more precarious. The strong are scattered in all directions, and the old and weak are relegated to the ditches. We hear of people eating bran and chaff, and smoke not rising from their chimneys. If this continues until this winter and next spring, the suffering will be unimaginable. Witnessing the current situation, we tremble with cold, and contemplating the future, our hearts are filled with extreme sorrow. We, the members of our association, have no way to stop this calamity, and our sins are great. Being at this dead end, we send out this urgent plea, daring to hope that benevolent gentlemen will show extra compassion and pity these hungry people with no one to turn to, and provide them with appropriate relief. This is what the 400,000 disaster-stricken people of Ying are reverently praying for.

Tao Xinfu and Liu Yangwen, President and Vice President of the Runhe Branch of the World Red Swastika Society, Ling Maolin, Wei Hanzhi, Ling Yunqin, Ling Liancai, Hu Kunpu, and all staff members, respectfully bow.

Chairman Chiang Directs the Enactment of Regulations for Compulsory Labor Service, Calling for Total Mobilization of People in All Provinces to Undertake Water Conservancy Projects, with Emphasis on Planting Trees and Constructing Roads 65

Chengdu Air Dispatch: Chairman Chiang issued a telegram on the 4th to military and political leaders of all provinces and cities, directing them to formulate regulations for compulsory labor service this winter, calling for total mobilization of the people in all provinces to undertake water conservancy projects and related construction. The original order is as follows: "To the Director of the Wuchang Headquarters, Chairmen of Provincial Governments, Mayors of Cities, Pacification Commissioners, and Commanders-in-Chief: It is recognized that labor is an innate human ability, and citizens especially should consider labor service as their natural duty. The accumulated neglect of construction in our country is due to insufficient financial resources and untapped human resources. Financial resources cannot be increased rapidly, but human resources are our advantage. By choosing the latter and teaching the people to work, we address the most urgent task of governance. If we can effectively encourage the people throughout the country to dedicate their spare time and energy annually to central tasks of the state and society as a form of service, then by maximizing human effort, we can ensure that land is fully utilized, resources are fully employed, and all matters are well-managed. I, Chairman Chiang, am deeply aware of this. Therefore, in April and December of last year, I sent telegrams to Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Henan, Hubei, Anhui, Jiangxi, Fujian, Hunan, Shaanxi, Gansu, Shanxi, Shandong, Chahar, Suiyuan, and Ningxia provinces, directing them to implement measures for compulsory labor service. In May of this year, I sent another telegram to Sichuan, Guizhou, and Yunnan provinces, instructing them to comply accordingly. However, some provinces have submitted draft outlines and implementation procedures for approval by the headquarters, while others have submitted outlines but not implementation procedures. Compliance is inconsistent, and the results are far from satisfactory. Considering the severe floods in both northern and southern provinces this year, and the widespread droughts in areas not affected by floods, the disasters are signs of inadequate human effort and neglected infrastructure. Rather than hastily providing relief after the event, it is better to prepare in advance. To concentrate efforts and address urgent needs, this winter's implementation of national labor service should involve total mobilization of the people in all provinces to jointly undertake water conservancy projects and related construction. The following outlines for compulsory labor service this winter are hereby established: (1) From November 1st of this year to March 31st of next year, shall be designated as the National Labor Service Water Conservancy Season. (2) The work during this season shall primarily focus on water conservancy projects such as dredging rivers, constructing embankments, repairing canals, and digging ponds, as well as afforestation and road construction. Trees should be planted along both sides of the roads. In flood-free areas with fewer water conservancy needs, emphasis should be placed on afforestation. (3) In addition to general citizens fulfilling their labor service obligations in accordance with regulations, all government officials at all levels and military officers and soldiers in the region must participate in labor service as an example. Faculty and students of secondary and higher education institutions should also complete ten days of labor service during their winter vacations. (4) Provincial and municipal governments should consider the actual local needs and prioritize the central tasks of their original policy outlines and the relevant water conservancy, afforestation, and road construction items within the people's labor service plans. The above-mentioned tasks should be the main focus during this season. However, within the same region, the order of priority for each task should be determined, and within the same task, the priority for each area should be clearly investigated and appropriately coordinated. Work should be organized by periods, areas, and groups, in accordance with the compulsory labor regulations. For area-based construction, attention should be paid to the connections of the entire project to ensure its effectiveness. Regulations for compulsory labor transfer between areas should be established to meet needs and ensure timely completion. (5) The conscription, allocation, and return of laborers should be handled with reference to the principles of conscription. (6) Before the end of October of this year, provincial and municipal governments should complete preparations for the necessary administrative and technical personnel and foremen needed for compulsory labor service this season. Training should be provided in personnel, technology, and management. Various engineering tools should be manufactured or purchased in advance to avoid delays due to lack of equipment. (7) Provincial and municipal governments should strictly regulate and enforce the supervision and assessment of administrative and technical staff, and the audit of tool usage. (8) Provincial and municipal governments should make every effort to economize on the expenses for this season's projects, and formulate their own methods for raising and disbursing funds. If it is truly impossible to raise funds or if the funds raised are insufficient, a portion may be drawn from the current year's reserve fund. (9) Before September 30th of this year, provincial and municipal governments should submit their complete compulsory labor service plans and budgets, along with all necessary charts, to the headquarters for approval and implementation in accordance with this outline. The above nine articles are to be strictly followed by the military and political leaders stationed in each province and city, and their subordinates. In short, utilizing existing labor to undertake essential projects is of great importance to national economic development. If the entire country can unite and actively promote this, the great benefits and rapid achievements can be confidently expected. However, this matter is of great importance. It is not difficult to gather laborers and start work, but it is difficult to plan and prepare. How to allocate resources based on the four factors of people, time, place, and task to ensure appropriateness? How to maximize efforts in guidance and supervision to improve work efficiency? It is hoped that these matters will be carefully considered and diligently implemented. Do not treat this as a mere formality. Chiang Chung-cheng. Secret dispatch from Rong (Central News Agency, September 8th)"

Praiseworthy Reputation of Young Artist Ma Sicong: Westerners in Hong Kong Enthusiastically Praise Ma's Pinnacle of Technical Skill 66

Hong Kong Correspondence: Mr. Ma Sicong, a great young Chinese artist in the music field, has long been highly regarded. He recently held a solo recital at the Hong Kong Hotel, attended by connoisseurs, amateur students, and music critics from various Western newspapers, creating a grand occasion. Mr. Ma is also a first-rate composer, with many of his scores published in Paris. This recital was originally intended to include his own sonata, but due to issues with the piano accompaniment, it was not possible. However, the performed pieces received enthusiastic praise from the audience. After the performance, the audience surrounded Mr. Ma, expressing their respect. Western newspapers also published separate reviews, praising him highly. For example, the South China Morning Post stated, "Violinist Ma Sicong held a recital at the Hong Kong Young Women's Christian Association in February of this year. He recently held another recital at the Hong Kong Hotel, attended by famous Chinese and Western musicians and amateur musicians. The program consisted entirely of Western music. Mr. Ma graduated from the highest art institute in Paris and has a clear understanding of Western music. His talent proves that Easterners have mastered Western music. Mr. Ma is a formidable young man with unlimited potential. It is difficult to predict the future of Eastern music or the extent to which Eastern and Western music will merge. However, Mr. Ma teaches at the National Central University in Nanjing and will continue to advance with his talent and enthusiasm. His future success can be foreseen. Mr. Ma's amazing technique can be seen in his strong bow control and accurate fingering. His volume, timbre, and tone are all perfectly controlled. Brahms' concerto is my favorite and can be called the most delightful score. Mr. Ma used his skillful technique to fully express the harmony of the violin in a solemn and gentle rhythm. In the performance of Tchaikovsky's concerto, Mr. Ma handled all the difficult techniques with ease. This piece is rarely attempted by famous musicians. Double stops require strength, and sautillé bowing requires extreme speed. Mr. Ma used his divine skill to achieve it effortlessly. The rest of the program gave us complete satisfaction in terms of technique and spirit. At the end of the program, the audience gave a warm round of applause, and we were even more delighted to hear an old melody of Louis XIII." The Hong Kong Telegraph stated, "Chinese young violinist Ma Sicong held his solo recital at the Hong Kong Hotel. Mr. Ma's use of the instrument, his rhythmic phrasing, and his skillful technique demonstrate his profound understanding of the meaning and value of music. The most valuable performance in the entire program was Tchaikovsky's concerto. From beginning to end, he was able to use his skillful technique to handle this rare and profound work. Technically speaking, he can be considered the pinnacle of violinists. The second movement in G major of Brahms' sonata is extremely beautiful in terms of the music itself, and it can be considered the first choice in the entire three movements. The author himself later had a sonata in D minor, both of which are excellent works. The violinist should be accurate with double stops (especially octaves), and the strength and clarity of the bow and the accuracy of the harmony can all show his level. Mr. Ma should be a great musician, I have no doubts. I hope Mr. Ma will have the opportunity to hold another recital, which I look forward to very much." The Hong Kong Weekly Press stated, "Mr. Ma Sicong performed various famous pieces at the Hong Kong Hotel on Monday evening, including extremely profound works. Was the audience able to fully understand the difficult performance techniques? I am confident that I understand. Before attending the recital, I thought that young Chinese musicians might not be able to fully mature in Western music, encompassing gentleness, strength, cleanliness, purity, and beauty. I am not overly praising Mr. Ma. It must be known that Mr. Ma's musical attainments, skilled performance, and profound emotions are due to his many years of education and training in Europe. Mr. Ma is twenty-three years old. He went to Paris at the age of eleven and studied there for seven years, receiving training from the famous teacher Bocher at the highest art institute in Paris. He returned to China in 1919 and was sponsored by the government to return to Europe in 1920 to specialize in composition. He is now a professor in the music department at the National Central University in Nanjing. Mr. Ma has composed many scores, and he promised to let me enjoy them, but his works are still in Shanghai. I hope to have the opportunity to appreciate them. Mr. Ma's sonata should be performed by three people. It was originally planned to be included in the program that evening, but the accompanist was not fully prepared, so it did not happen. Therefore, people in Hong Kong who want to listen to Mr. Ma's works must wait for another day. This sonata is not an ordinary score, but it can evoke a pleasant mood." The sincere publicity given to Mr. Ma by various Western newspapers in Hong Kong shows the high level of his art, which can move people.

Baoshan: Construction Begins on Jiangnan Seawall 67

The Jiangnan seawall stretches for over 500 li, starting from Changshu, passing through Taicang, Baoshan, Chuansha, Nanhui, Fengxian, Songjiang, and ending in Jinshan. It is the guarantee of life and property for more than ten coastal counties. Except for Fengxian, Chuansha, and Nanhui counties, where the beaches outside the seawall are quite wide and the situation is relatively calm, the four counties of Bao, Tai, Song, and Chang are situated on the river and sea, and are particularly dangerous. In light of the severe floods and disasters in various provinces this year, the Jiangnan Water Conservancy Engineering Office, fearing that the dangerous sections of the seawall would be flooded, appointed Mr. Liu Yeqiu to oversee the construction to prevent any eventuality. After receiving the order, Director Liu immediately established an office in Baoshan and actively planned and carried out the work. It is reported that offices in various sections have also been established, and construction has now started in all sections. Barring unforeseen circumstances, the work should be completed in two months.

Suzhou: Hurricane Hits Suzhou, Roofs Blown Away 68

The weather in Suzhou has been exceptionally hot recently, with temperatures consistently above 90 degrees on the thermometer. As a result, centipedes have appeared in the rice fields in the countryside, causing the seedlings to wither and turn yellow. The autumn harvest will be severely damaged. The villagers have reported the disaster to the county government. County Magistrate Wu has ordered the heads of various rural districts to conduct thorough investigations in order to submit a report to the provincial government for approval. On the 12th, around noon, a sudden strong wind blew, sand covered the faces, and the weather changed dramatically. People felt cold in their summer clothes, as if it were late autumn. Spirits were refreshed. Around 3 PM, the hurricane had not stopped. Many telephone poles were blown down in the city and suburbs. Countless awnings and other objects were blown away. Some tile roofs were also blown down.

Furthermore, the Yuantiao Guan Zhongyou Hall, which was built on the old site of the Luogong Building with local funding, was completed on April 4th of last year. It has a Roman-style dome, which is magnificent. The first group wedding in Suzhou, scheduled to be held during the Double Tenth Festival, was planned to be held in this hall. At 12:55 PM on the 12th, a sudden hurricane blew away the entire roof. The solid top of the central conference room was even blown into a hole, measuring 15 meters in length and 11 meters in width. The beam in the middle was also broken. The bricks and tiles were blown onto the floor. Fortunately, no one was inside, so no one was injured. The four characters "Tian Xia Wei Gong" (The World is for All) above the front of the hall were also smashed. As it was the Mid-Autumn Festival, there were many tourists in the temple. The county party headquarters and the Wu County government heard the news and went to the scene to investigate. Around 1 PM, the west wall continued to collapse. According to the Suzhou Meteorological Station of the Yangtze River Water Conservancy Commission, the wind was a southwest wind, with a force of six. At 2 PM, it had not subsided. The pressure at 12 PM was 755.97 mm, and it rose to 757.54 mm at 2 PM. The temperature was 91 degrees at 12 PM, and it dropped to 76 degrees at 2 PM.

Wuxi: New Autumn Cocoons Hit the Market Yesterday 69

The 12th was the first day of weighing and trading of autumn cocoons in the four rural areas of this county. The goods arriving were very enthusiastic, but the cocoons were not in good condition. The Gongtailong cocoon shop in Sitouzhen, District 5, received 25 yuan per load of cocoons. However, the scales they used were still the old system and had not been replaced with new scales. Therefore, the villagers there expressed dissatisfaction and gathered to cause trouble, destroying the wooden fences of the shop. The owner of the shop, seeing that the situation was not good, immediately reported to the Public Security Bureau, which sent police to suppress the situation. The matter was then settled. The output of fresh autumn cocoons in the four rural areas this year is estimated to be 76,000 piculs, equivalent to 23,700 piculs of dry cocoons. The Wuxi Cocoon Industry Association, fearing that speculative cocoon shops would take advantage of the autumn cocoon market to acquire unpaid cocoons at high prices, harming farmers, specially requested the county government to issue a strict prohibition.

Yangzhou: Robbery Occurs on Xiao Zhi Ma Lane 70

Lu Dejiu, a resident of Xiaozhizhima Lane in the city, is currently working at the Guide River Project Office. Letter to the Editor 75

To the esteemed Editor of Shen Bao,

The article "Pear Peel Causes Trouble, Police Officer Injured" in your Jiading local news section on September 11th does not conform to the facts. According to a report from the Zhouqiao patrol station chief, Hu Jun, on the 9th of this month, at 5:20 PM on this day, police officer Chen Yangjie saw an employee of the Yichang Water Store throwing pear cores on the street, which was detrimental to hygiene. He ordered the employee to pick them up. Zhu Fuquan, an employee of Yichangyong, refused to comply and cursed the police officer on the spot. After the police officer warned him, Zhu Fuquan gathered several dozen of his fellow employees and neighbors and shouted, "Beat him!" They dragged the police officer into the store, tied him up, beat him, tore his uniform, and left him covered in injuries. He requested immediate rescue. In order to avoid escalating the situation, the bureau immediately dispatched patrol officers Zhuo Dengwen, Liu Debiao, and Huang Xiwang to investigate and resolve the matter and maintain order. It was later reported that the police officers who arrived at the scene were also beaten and injured and returned to the bureau in a disheveled state, requesting an examination. At the same time, similar incidents occurred in the southwest parts of the city, causing disorder and unrest. Fortunately, the county government dispatched a security team to suppress the situation and strengthened the city's defenses, quickly restoring the original state. The injured police officers and the destroyed documents have been sent to the county government for investigation and handling. The article published in your newspaper is likely based on inaccurate rumors. We are sending this letter to request a correction and express our gratitude.

Respectfully,

Jiading County Public Security Bureau

Commercial Organizations in Jiangsu Province Seek to Revive Native Cloth Industry, Petition to Establish a Department to Find Ways to Provide Relief, Loan Funds to Farmers to Purchase Looms 83

Commercial organizations throughout Jiangsu Province, in view of the increasing decline of the native cloth industry in recent years, and fearing that the future is extremely dangerous if no measures are taken to provide relief, specially resolved by commercial organizations throughout the province to petition the Construction Department for relief. The original petition is as follows: "The reason for the decline of industry and commerce in our country is that the only problem lies in the lack of a sound regulatory policy, which has caused a tragic decline whenever superior foreign goods are encountered. Think about how in recent years, people in and out of the government in our country have been advocating domestic goods, and it can be said that their efforts have been exhausted, but the result is only a large number of inferior goods flooding the market. With foreign goods flooding in, the Chinese people should set up factories to stop the leaks, but the result is the opposite. They only see the path of following the trend, neglecting the important task of promoting domestic goods and blocking leaks, and will inevitably be eliminated. In order to prevent domestic goods from undercutting each other in the market, which has led to the decline of domestic goods, it is necessary to implement regulation without delay. Since the dumping of foreign goods, native cloth has gradually disappeared, and factories using power looms have risen at the right time, so that factory cloth is no less than a substitute for native cloth, and foreign goods are given a great opportunity. The failure of the silk industry is beyond salvation, and there are no less than hundreds of thousands of farmers who rely on this weaving sideline for their livelihood. The annual output of woven cloth by the industry associations is more than 1.5 million pieces, which is equivalent to more than 10 million yuan in national currency. It is closely related to the national economy and the people's livelihood. In the face of tight finances, material difficulties, and precarious operations, in addition to the thorough ban on night work to save the current crisis, looking ahead, there is no optimism. After joint discussions, it was unanimously agreed that only by carrying out regulatory methods can the crisis be saved. It is clear that without thoroughness, a good plan cannot be realized. The only way is to request the government to formulate the general outline of the regulatory system as soon as possible, order the various industries to formulate detailed rules, and submit them for approval, and supervise their implementation within a time limit, so that the country's future can be revitalized. As for artificial weaving, it has been affected by the intrusion of foreign goods over the years, and has been reduced year by year. Recently, although hand-pulled wooden looms have been used to widen and lengthen the front, the number of pieces woven each day is not large. In order to restore farmers' sideline occupations, it is planned to use foot-operated iron looms to increase patterns and increase production. However, farmers are limited by economic power to buy iron and wood looms, which cost about 50 yuan each, and it is difficult to prepare them. It is proposed to develop assistance measures, that is, to ask your department to consult with the Provincial Farmers' Bank, and order the branches in each county to loan 50,000 yuan in national currency to the cooperative societies and rural offices in the cloth-producing areas to be loaned to farmers, with a limit of 50 yuan per household, for the purchase of looms, or the Farmers' Bank will purchase 1,000 iron and wood looms, which will be transferred to farmers by cooperative societies and rural offices in the cloth-producing areas, one loom per household, and 10 yuan will be repaid each year, and the loan will be paid off in five years. Farmers will benefit from the assistance, and the output can be viewed. In the future, the surplus from wages can be used to purchase more looms year by year, and neighboring farmers can also follow suit. In this way, on the one hand, the rural sideline occupations can be revived, and on the other hand, the livelihood of farmers can be enriched and the skills of our country's native cloth weaving can be transformed, and the intrusion of foreign goods can be resisted invisibly and the huge leaks can be stopped."

Yi Li General Company Operated by Xu Yanzuo Ceased Operations Yesterday, Public Soda Water, Glass, Shipping, and Hardware Businesses Entrusted to Lawyers and Accountants for Liquidation 86

Xin Sheng She reported that Yi Li General Company at 33 Tianjin Road, affected by the closure of Sanmen Bay Real Estate and Mei Feng Bank, suffered from financial difficulties and was unable to maintain operations. Yesterday, the general company and its affiliated soda factory, glass factory, shipping company, hardware store, real estate company, and bank all ceased operations at the same time and entrusted accountant Jiang Xinzhao and others to liquidate. Details are as follows:

Businesses Operated by Xu Tingzuo

Yi Li General Company was founded by Xu Tingzuo from Dinghai as a sole proprietorship with a total capital of more than 1 million yuan in national currency. The businesses include Yi Li Soda Factory (address: 1568 Huade Road), Yi Li Hardware Store (address: 74 Broadway), Yi Li Shipping Company (address: 33 Tianjin Road), Yi Li Glass Factory (address: 1568 Huade Road), Zhen Li Bank (address: 170 Broadway), and Sanmen Bay Real Estate Company. It has its own Yi Li and Yi Tai ships that operate on the Shanghai-Wenzhou line and also acts as an agent for Yi Sun Shipping Company's Yi Sun ship. Business has been quite prosperous and the reputation is excellent. Xu Tingzuo serves as the general manager, and Xu Wengui, He Jinyun, Qin Rongquan, and others serve as managers of various factories and stores.

Failure to Reclaim Sanmen Bay

Xu Tingzuo aspired to reclaim Sanmen Bay, hoping to develop it into a commercial port. He invested 300,000 to 400,000 yuan successively to purchase beach land and invited people from all walks of life in Shanghai to visit Sanmen Bay. At the same time, the Yi Li ship was also used to transport to Sanmen Bay for the purpose of developing Sanmen Bay. Unfortunately, since the Northeast Incident and the Shanghai War broke out one after another, the political situation was unstable and the government had no time to pay attention to this. At the same time, no one in the society responded, resulting in all the investment being stranded, consuming more than 400,000 yuan for land prices. This is what Xu feels most painful about.

Excessive Losses and Financial Difficulties

The shipping division, namely Yi Li Shipping Company's Yi Li ship, has a total tonnage of 1,055 tons and a net tonnage of 618 tons. The Yi Sun ship, which is an agency, has a total tonnage of 1,833 tons and a net tonnage of 1,068 tons. Since the opening of the route, business has been sluggish and losses have reached more than 200,000 yuan. In addition to the failure to develop Sanmen Bay, the vitality has been greatly damaged and finances have become tight. At the same time, the entire industrial and commercial atmosphere in Shanghai has reached its extreme. The banking industry has tightened loans of all kinds. The company tried its best to reorganize in order to survive.

Unable to Maintain Operations and Forced to Close

Since the closure of American Mei Feng Bank for liquidation, Yi Li General Company had overdraft transactions and owed more than 400,000 yuan. Interest was paid on time and there was no problem. Since the closure of the bank, the principal of the above overdraft, although not yet due, was urgently recovered. Although the company's assets were more than enough to compensate, the capital had been converted into real estate, factory buildings, machinery, and inventory. No one could take over at one time, and the receivables could not be recovered urgently, resulting in huge amounts of cash that could not be raised. Depositors rushed to withdraw funds, resulting in the inability to maintain operations, and the general company and its affiliated factories and stores had to be closed for liquidation.

Entrusted to Lawyers to Announce Liquidation

Yesterday, at the entrance of the general company, lawyers He Baiqian and accountant Jiang Xinzhao, representing the company, announced, "It is now reported by the person in charge of Yi Li Company that Yi Li Soda Factory, Yi Li Glass Factory, Yi Li Yi Sun Shipping Bureau, and Yi Li Hardware Store are affected by the market and cannot maintain operations due to financial difficulties. We have been entrusted to represent the liquidation. Therefore, we hereby announce on behalf of the company that all creditors are requested to bring their vouchers within 14 days to register at the liquidation office for verification. All debtors are also requested to send the owed funds to the liquidation office within the above-mentioned period to obtain receipts. If the deadline is exceeded, legal action will be taken. This is hereby notified. Liquidation Office: 170 Broadway.

Xu's Attitude is Very Negative

Xu Tingzuo is from Dinghai, Zhejiang, and is 54 years old. In view of the influx of foreign goods and the outflow of rights and interests, he has worked hard to establish industries to stop the leaks. In 1927, he founded Yi Li Soda Factory as a sole proprietorship, producing various sodas and orange juice. The sales are very wide and comparable to imported products. He purchased ships such as Yi Li to operate on the Shanghai-Wenzhou and Hong Kong-Guangzhou lines. He set up a hardware store to promote canned food and jointly formed Zhen Li Bank with Deng Zhenquan. He usually has no hobbies and takes starting a business as a pastime. He is praised by the people of Shanghai and is a member of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce's Committee for the Promotion of Domestic Goods. This sudden setback is unfulfilled and is extremely negative. It is reported that he is still staying in Shanghai, but he is refusing visitors.

Setting Up a Liquidation Office to Handle Registration

The Yi Li Soda Factory, Yi Li Hardware Store, Yi Li Shipping Company, Yi Li Glass Factory, Zhen Li Bank, and Sanmen Bay Real Estate Company, which are affiliated with the general company, have all closed down. Ships such as Yi Li have stopped sailing and are anchored on the Huangpu River in Gaochangmiao. The seafarers, factory workers, and store employees, totaling about several thousand people, have all become unemployed. The lawyers and accountants who are now handling the liquidation have set up a liquidation office at 170 Broadway to handle registration.

Assets and Liabilities are Very Close

Yesterday, the Xin Sheng She reporter learned from accountant Jiang Xinzhao that the total assets of Yi Li Company, such as real estate, factory buildings, machinery, inventory, and receivables, together with the two ships Yi Li and Yi Sun, are worth about 1.1 million yuan. The total amount of liabilities is estimated to be more than 2.3 million yuan, most of which are Mei Feng and other current accounts, a small number are consignment transactions, and individual deposits from relatives and friends. After offsetting each other, the difference is about 200,000 yuan. Except for most of the debts being secured by ships and factory buildings, the value of the collateral is also surplus. Therefore, the actual difference is negligible.

Decided to Discuss Reopening Methods

Xu's operation of various businesses was affected by the depression in the market and was unfortunately unable to turn around and was forced to close down. It is reported that after the accounts are cleared and settled, a meeting of creditors will be convened to discuss everything and then prepare to resume operations in order to fulfill the original intention of striving to start an industry.

US Consulate Issues Shanghai's Exports to the US in August 87

Da Mei Evening News reports that the US Consulate General in Shanghai issued today (the 12th) statistics on Shanghai's exports to the United States, the Philippines, and Hawaii in August. The total value of exports to the US was US$1,239,479, a significant increase compared to the total value of US$1,005,215 in July and the total value of US$714,524 in August last year. In the first eight months of this year, Shanghai's exports to the US totaled US$2,013,662, compared to only US$7,935,906 in the same period last year. Shanghai's exports to the Philippines continued to decline, with US$81,247 in July and US$78,068 in August, compared to US$113,560 in the same period last year. In the first eight months of this year, the total value was US$648,057, compared to US$841,669 in the same period last year. Shanghai's exports to Hawaii increased from US$1,756 in July to US$2,381 in August, but decreased compared to US$4,933 in August last year. In the first eight months of this year, the total value was US$30,123, compared to US$33,709 in the same period last year. In August this year, Shanghai's exports to the US were led by textiles, totaling US$598,510, compared to US$371,952 in the same month last year, followed by inedible plant products, totaling US$35,450, and then inedible animal and animal products, totaling US$186,7881. However, this type of item actually ranked first in the total value of Shanghai's exports to the US in the first eight months of this year, totaling US$3,5221,622, which was still a decrease compared to US$4,086,934 in the same period last year. Textiles exported to the US in the first eight months of this year totaled US$3,376,277, compared to only US$619,285 in the same period last year, a significant increase.

Five Reefs Discovered in the Lower Reaches of the Yangtze River, the Survey Bureau Sent the Qingtian Warship to Conduct a Survey, Naming the Two Stones and Notifying the Navigation Industry to Pay Attention 88

Datong News Agency reports that according to the Hydrographic Survey Bureau of the Ministry of the Navy in this city, five reefs have been discovered in the Dongliu Channel (south of Tianxin Island) in the lower reaches of the Yangtze River, from Anqing to Jiujiang. Among them, the area of both is quite large, exposing 2 to 3 feet above the water surface, and the area of the remaining three is smaller, ranging from 10 to 32 feet below the water surface. Now, the bureau has sent the Qingtian Survey Ship to complete the survey. It has been found that the nature of the two largest areas is completely reef, and the three smaller areas are stone seabed. According to the size of the area, five kinds of notations are listed, namely A, B, C, D, and E, all of which are planned to be named Liang Stones. The longitude and latitude are 116 degrees 50 minutes east longitude and about 20 degrees 8 minutes north latitude, and the Chinese and foreign shipping pilots have been notified to pay attention.
