The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Telegraphed the Ministry of Finance to Order the Customs to Return the Jade Rough, The Paid Fines Were Detained Again, and Repeated Appeals Have Not Been Approved 92

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce reported that Chen Kaiqing, a Yunnan merchant, transported jade rough to Shanghai and was penalized by the customs for underreporting the price. After paying the full amount, the goods were detained again by the customs. Four months have passed, and the Chamber has repeatedly telegraphed the Customs Administration and the Ministry of Finance, but has not received approval. It is hereby telegraphed again to request a prompt return. The repeated telegrams are recorded below:

Telegraph to the Customs Administration

To the Customs Administration of the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing, the merchant Chen Kaiqing transported jade rough from Myanmar to Shanghai on April 21. He declared the goods according to the original price, but the customs considered the declared price to be lower than the assessed price. In addition to paying taxes according to the assessed price, he was also fined three times. He paid the full amount on April 29 and took the goods back. While he was working on the stones, the customs took the goods away and detained them on May 22, saying that someone reported that the value of the item was quite large and needed to be investigated and dealt with. Otherwise, a guarantee must be paid in advance before it can be returned. The merchant has repeatedly stated to the customs that the business has been assessed for tax and the penalty has been completed, and there should be no further complications. Please order the customs to return the original item. He has also asked to forward the telegram here. It is found that for goods with assessed prices and taxes, the merchant who considers the assessment to be too high can raise objections within a certain period. As for the customs, since the law gives it the power to assess prices, it should be prudent in advance. According to the current regulations, the customs does not seem to have the right to raise objections to the tax that has been assessed and paid. Let's take a step back, even if such a disposal is necessary, a considerable period should be stipulated, and the expiration date should be determined. In this case, the merchant has already paid the tax according to the assessment and paid the fine. The execution has been completed and the case has been closed. In terms of judicial events, even if the prosecutor believes that the court's punishment is too light, he must file an appeal within the appeal period. There is no reason to overturn the case at any time after the execution has been completed. According to the previous situation, after paying the tax and the penalty, the merchant still cannot process, manufacture, sell, or transport the goods, and may be subject to re-evaluation and detention at any time. The right is always in an uncertain state. In terms of law and reason, there is no such method. Please quickly telegraph the Shanghai Customs, so as not to make unfounded demands on this closed case, and return the goods to Chen Kaiqing for collection as soon as possible. I pray, Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce (sent on July 17) (2) To the Ministry of Finance of Nanjing, the Customs Administration, in the case of Chen Kaiqing's jade rough, the merchant submitted a report to your office in May, and the Chamber of Commerce telegraphed it again, but has not received a reply. It is a matter of course to pay taxes according to the assessed price, and the goods that have been penalized have been detained for several months without being released, which makes merchants and people have no guarantee. The Commissioner of Customs replied to the merchant that the case has been handled by the Customs Administration, and that the power to dispose of this matter fairly lies with your office. I hope you will check the telegraph and deal with it quickly to alleviate the burden on the merchants. Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce (sent on July 31)

Report to the Ministry of Finance

Report for the matter of requesting. According to Yunnan merchant Chen Kaiqing, on April 21, jade rough was transported from Myanmar to Shanghai for sale. He declared the goods according to the original price, but the customs considered the declared price to be lower than the assessed price. In addition to paying taxes according to the assessed price, he was also fined three times. He paid the full amount on April 29 and took the goods back. On May 22, the customs took the goods away and detained them, saying that someone reported that the value of the item was quite large and needed to be investigated and dealt with. Otherwise, a guarantee must be paid in advance before it can be returned. The merchant has repeatedly stated to the customs that the business has been assessed for tax and the penalty has been completed, and there should be no further complications. Please order the return of the original item. The merchant also submitted a report to the Customs Administration, but did not receive approval. Please provide assistance. The Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Customs Administration on July 17, stating that if the merchant considers the tax too high, he can raise objections within a certain period. If the customs has been given full power to assess prices by law, it should be prudent in advance and should not pick on things after the fact. Moreover, in this case, the merchant has paid the tax according to the assessed price and paid the fine. The execution has been completed, and the merchant has the full right to process, manufacture, sell, and transport the goods. If it is re-evaluated and detained at any time, the right is always in an uncertain state. According to laws and reason, there is no such method. Please correct the Shanghai Customs quickly. It has been a long time since I have received a reply. The Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Customs Administration on July 31, requesting a quick handling, but it is still being shelved. As such, the merchant's business has been suspended for a long time, which is not only a loss, but also no different from a double penalty for one case, which has never happened before. I have prepared a document to submit to your department, hoping that you will examine it and order the Customs Administration to order the Shanghai Customs to return the detained goods to the merchant for collection, so as to conform to the principles of fairness. I am sincerely grateful. (Sent on August 17)

Telegraph to the Ministry of Finance

To the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing, the case of Chen Kaiqing's jade rough has been assessed for tax and the penalty has been completed by the customs, but it has been detained for several months due to other complications. The customs has not taken any reasonable measures. I had to telegraph the Customs Administration on July 30, and on August 10, I submitted another report to your department. It has been more than a month, but I have not received an order to return the goods. It has never happened before that a case that has been determined and closed has been dragged on for so long. I respectfully request that you order the release as soon as possible. Thank you very much. Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce (sent on September 11)

New Jiangtian Ferryboat Workers Submit New Life Training Opinions; Yesterday Jointly Submitted to China Merchants Bureau for Adoption 100

The New Jiangtian ferryboat of the state-run China Merchants Bureau recently received an order from the Nanchang New Life Movement General Association to hold a New Life Training Class for tea-room staff, and 120 people were selected to go ashore first to start training. The tea-room staff remaining on the boat jointly submitted their opinions to the China Merchants Bureau, requesting their adoption. The original text reads, "Your Majesty, in order to contribute opinions, we sincerely request that you adopt and implement the matter. We, the entire staff of the boat, have been serving passengers for more than 20 years. In the past, for all kinds of facilities that benefit the business of the Bureau or the successive managers of the boat, we did not dare to express any opposition even if we suffered great harm. That is, the General Manager resolutely reorganized the boat this time, first re-registering, taking photos and inspecting, examining the physique, seeking guarantees, filling in voluntary books, etc., all followed orders. Unexpectedly, soon after, the boat staff were ordered to draw lots and transfer 120 people ashore to receive New Life training. The staff recognized that the General Manager's plan was profound, and after receiving the order, they worried that the boat staff were too old to undergo military training, and that the blind, weak, and old tea servants could not pass the training in a short period of time in other literacy, writing letters, and dialect classes. Therefore, without waiting for the lottery, they automatically agreed to first select 120 older people and secretly submit the list to listen to the training. The staff's move was actually to wait for the first batch of trained graduates to return to the boat and then request the General Manager to implement the small teacher system, training the first batch of trained and qualified people to train the remaining 140 people on the boat. This will not only make it easier for the staff to receive popular education, but also reduce the burden on the Bureau. I think the General Manager has the mission of reorganizing the business development of the China Merchants Bureau's ships. The above-mentioned idea of achieving two goals with one move should be adopted. Furthermore, according to the current situation of our China Merchants Bureau, if the tea servants of all the ships under its jurisdiction are given wages by the Bureau, as in the case of this boat, to win the hearts of passengers and expand business development, in the opinion of the staff, it is not a good strategy. This is because the shipping routes to various places are not exclusively for the Bureau's passengers to travel back and forth, and it is not necessarily because the staff of the Bureau's ships do not charge for wine that they can increase the number of passengers. Then, the passengers who increase on our boat must be greedy for cheap prices. If other companies therefore feel that the reduction in passengers affects their business, they will also rise up and imitate to resist. If they send more gifts and implement individual cheap and expensive prices to compete for business, we will not only lack benefits to gain, but the result will inevitably be a lose-lose situation. The staff, having learned from this, has presented the above-mentioned views for the future of the Bureau's business, and proposes to uniformly follow the order to extract wine money from the tea rooms of all ships, which can reduce the burden of more than 600,000 yuan and avoid resentment from other ships. Whether it is appropriate, we have prepared a document to request your approval and implementation, in the spirit of public service. Respectfully presented to General Manager Liu of the China Merchants Bureau, respectfully presented by all the staff of the New Jiangtian ferryboat."

The runaway carriage was caused by flies patting the horse's feet; the horse went wild and the belly band broke; all injuries will be compensated 105

At 2:10 PM the other day, on Hua Fa Min Guo Road, Lao Bei Men, there was a carriage of the French Public Works Bureau, No. 5, without a driver, causing it to run wild. It sped to Xiao Bei Men, knocking down rickshaws and pedestrians along the way, as well as the driver of public bus No. 315, Lu Qingshan, and others, a total of thirteen men, women, and children, mostly suffering from trampling, falling injuries, and injuries to the head, legs, waist, shoulders, arms, and feet. It has been reported in this newspaper that the police chief Shen sent them to the hospital for treatment. It is learned that Chief Shen, in order to arrange for the medical expenses and loss of property of the injured, sent Officer Ma to the French Public Works Bureau to investigate. It was found that the carriage was not lost due to negligence. The carriage was parked at the Lao Bei Men on that day, and flies were stinging the horse's feet, making it uneasy. The groom was patting the flies, but for some reason, the horse suddenly went wild. The belly band broke, and the groom was kicked down and seriously injured while trying to control the horse, resulting in the runaway. All injury expenses will be compensated. Officer Ma returned to the station to report, and the report was submitted to the Bureau for verification and handling.

Patent for Silver Light Bulbs Is Challenged 106

For several months, among the types of light bulbs on the market, "Silver Light Bulbs" have emerged. It is claimed to be invented by a Chinese gentleman and has been granted a patent by the government, causing quite a stir. Recently, Wang Meiqing filed an objection with the government regarding the patent, stating that the so-called Silver Light Bulbs were manufactured in Belgium long ago and named the Albo brand. They were tested at the National Testing Institute of Leuven, Belgium on June 9, 1934, and again at the Central Electrical Testing Institute of Paris on August 14. Both have supporting documents. Mr. Wang has sent photos of these supporting documents to the Ministry for verification.

Private Trafficking and Drug Use; Jiang Sixing and Xu Caoshi Await Sentencing 108

Xu Shutian, a Chinese detective of the Huishan Patrol Room, and Chinese patrolman No. 1838, found Jiang Si, a native of Anhui, acting suspiciously on Dongyouheng Road at around 1 PM the day before yesterday. They stopped him and found two small bags of opium and fifty red pills on his person. When questioned, he confessed that the contraband items were given to him by Wang Qinglin, a native of Jiangxi at No. 95 on the same road, to sell on his behalf. Detective Xu secretly went to the address and arrested Wang on the third floor of the house. A Jiangbei woman, Xu Caoshi (Wang's mistress), was also arrested. She had a satisfied look on her face, a copper cigarette holder in her mouth, and was smoking heroin to satisfy her addiction. A pack of red pills, totaling ten pills, was also found under the pillow of the bed. All were taken to the patrol room, detained separately, and sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court the next morning. Mr. Li Zhishan, a lawyer of the Public Works Bureau, stated the case and requested prosecution. Subsequently, Detective Xu and Patrolman No. 1838 reported the progress of the case and presented the evidence for inspection. When questioned, Jiang Sixing confessed that Wang Qinglin was the main culprit, but Wang firmly denied it, claiming that he had a grudge against Jiang Sixing and was being falsely accused. He claimed to live downstairs in the house and that the seized evidence belonged to someone else. Xu Caoshi claimed that she picked up the cigarette butt, which was not heroin, from the road. Judge Jiang Shuzi ordered them to be remanded in custody separately and scheduled sentencing.

Yesterday, Judge Jiang Shuzi opened the Third Criminal Court for interrogation. Mr. Li Zhishan, a lawyer of the Public Works Bureau, explained the previous situation and stated that no other cases had been found in the meantime. He requested severe punishment according to the law. Subsequently, the victims filed cases, proving the circumstances of the robbery by the defendants at the time. When questioned, Ren Jingchu confessed that a certain Jia, who was at large, had initiated the robbery. Jiang Dingxiu denied it, while Yang Fulin and Li Mingsheng gave evasive confessions. Judge Jiang ordered them to be remanded in custody and await sentencing.

Cao Rongqing Lost His Life Due to Coal Baskets; Died Suddenly After Unintentionally Receiving Stolen Goods 110

Cao Rongqing (60 years old), a native of Chuansha, opened the Cao Shunxing bamboo shop in Miezhu Street, Nanshi, offering all kinds of bamboo utensils. Since its opening, it has been more than 30 years, and the business has been doing well. However, the shop has never had any workers. The source of its bamboo products has always been from Suzhou and other places, where boats are hired to load them into Shanghai for sale to customers. At around 7 AM, a certain Jia, carrying twelve large coal baskets, came to the Cao Shunxing shop to sell them. Cao Rongqing came out to negotiate, offering three jiao per basket, for a total of three yuan and six jiao. After the deal was made, Jia left with the money. After Cao Rongqing bought the baskets, Lao Yu, who runs the Yu Yongxing bamboo shop in Chenjia Bridge, Nanshi, suddenly arrived at Cao's shop and claimed that he wanted to buy the twelve large coal baskets. Cao Rongqing pointed out the large coal baskets he had just bought and asked him to inspect them. They agreed on a price of six jiao per basket. Lao Yu asked Cao to deliver the goods to the Chenjia Bridge shop to collect the money. Cao did not suspect anything and happily hired a cart to load the coal baskets and escorted them there. Unexpectedly, when passing the Chenjia Bridge Police Station, Lao Yu reported to the guard, pointing out that the coal baskets were stolen goods that he had lost and claiming that thefts had been frequent among the same trade recently, requesting a thorough investigation. The station detained Cao Rongqing and the coal baskets and sent them to the Ximen Branch Bureau. Cao Rongqing's son, Cao Gentao, claimed that the coal baskets had been brought by Jia, who had been introduced by Xia Jusheng, the owner of the Yiji bamboo shop at the intersection of Shachang Street, Miezhu Street, stating that they were goods from a closed shop and should be sold for cash. Since the dispute had arisen, Xia Jusheng could not stay out of it. He immediately negotiated with Xia Xuesheng and went to the police station to collect evidence and file a loss report, requesting a thorough investigation. Unexpectedly, Cao Rongqing suddenly fell ill in custody. His condition was very serious. With the approval of Chief Li, he was sent to the Shanghai Hospital for treatment. The rest of the matter was reported to the Third Section of the Public Security Bureau for investigation. Cao Rongqing's illness was said to be a stroke, and there was no way to save him. He died in the hospital at 9:10 PM that night. The local headman, Gu Juyuan, reported the death to the local court yesterday, requesting an autopsy. Subsequently, Cao Rongqing's son, Cao Gentao, submitted a petition to the court requesting exemption from the autopsy and offering to arrange the coffin and burial himself. He was instructed to wait for further instructions.

Loan Committee Guides the Procedure for Filling Out Promissory Notes 111

The Shanghai Industry and Commerce Loan Review Committee has held meetings and approved multiple credit microloans. The committee has been notifying the applicants one after another to go to the China National Products Bank on Tianjin Road to receive the loans. The bank has been very busy handling the loans, and many applicants do not fill out the promissory notes and term bills according to the original procedure, resulting in frequent errors and requiring them to be filled out again. In order to facilitate the loan recipients and avoid procedural errors, the Loan Committee has specially stipulated that each loan recipient, upon receiving the approval notice, can go to the bank for blank promissory notes and term bills. If there are any unclear filling procedures, they can go directly to the Loan Committee office upstairs in the bank to consult in person. The committee will send staff to guide them in detail, complete the procedures, and then go to the bank to receive the loan. This will avoid procedural errors and save them from traveling back and forth. Loan recipients are advised to pay attention.

The Ministry of Finance Approves the Prohibition of Counterfeit Soy Sauce in Five Provinces; Products Not Made with Salt Sauce Cannot Be Called Soy Sauce 112

The trade associations of the soy sauce industry in the five provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Hubei previously discovered that tax-evading and toxic counterfeit soy sauce was being sold in various regions, harming businesses, affecting national revenue, and endangering people's livelihoods. They convened a joint meeting and petitioned the Ministry of Finance and the Salt Affairs Administration in Beijing. Yesterday, they received a response from the Ministry of Finance, which stated in its original text: "Ministry of Finance Salt Character No. 697, reply to the petition from the representatives of the trade associations of the soy sauce industry in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Hubei." The petition concerned black tax, toxic counterfeit soy sauce being sold in various regions, and requested that the ban be reiterated, the order to prohibit it be issued, and a notice be issued prohibiting the mixing of soy sauce and the old names of various soy sauce gardens. The Salt Affairs Administration reviewed the petition and presented it. The Ministry of Finance ordered the relevant salt affairs management agencies to investigate and prohibit any seasoning products not made with salt sauce from being mixed with soy sauce, soy sauce essence, or other names similar to soy sauce. A public notice should be issued to inform the public, to promote the sale of authentic soy sauce and increase salt tax revenue. The notice was issued, Minister Kong Xiangxi.

Collision Between a Chinese Tram and a French Tram at the Intersection of Ximen and Heping Road Yesterday; Chinese Tram Derailed but French Tram Remained Operable 114

At 3:30 PM yesterday at the intersection of Ximen and Heping Road, Tram No. 44 of the China General Edison Company, traveling from Sanyuan Road to Minguo Road in Ximen City, heading north, collided with a French-owned tram traveling from Minguo Road to Sanlu Road, which was exiting Ximen and proceeding to the five-route tram station, turning onto the straight track. The collision caused the Chinese tram to derail and completely damage its transmission shaft. The French tram remained operable. The China General Edison Company dispatched a rescue vehicle to put the derailed tram back on the rails. Trams from routes 2 and 4 were used to tow the damaged tram to the company for repairs, resulting in losses of approximately 200 yuan. The French tram was able to proceed. The accident blocked traffic, affecting about twenty Chinese and French trams for about half an hour.

Shanghai Experienced Sudden Rain After Extreme Heat Yesterday; Weather Changed Drastically and Temperature Dropped Suddenly; Temperature Difference of About 20 Degrees in One Day; High Pressure from the West Affected the Entire Country 115

Shanghai experienced consecutive days of extreme heat and abnormal weather. From 11:00 AM to 12:00 PM yesterday, the weather was particularly dry and stuffy. Although it was already mid-Autumn, the temperature still exceeded 95 degrees. However, at 1:30 PM, dark clouds suddenly gathered, followed by a torrential downpour, which was particularly severe in the central concession area. By 2:30 PM, there had been four or five waves of rain, with a total rainfall of half a foot. Low-lying areas throughout the city were flooded. The temperature dropped from 95 degrees to 88.5 degrees. After 3:00 PM, the rain subsided slightly, and the temperature dropped further to 77.5 degrees. The temperature difference in one day was about 20 degrees. It is reported that the sudden change in weather yesterday was caused by the arrival of high pressure from the west, causing sudden cold weather in central provinces across the country, especially in the north. Qingdao experienced a northerly wind of force 9, while Yantai experienced a north-northwesterly wind of force 9 or higher. The weather in the upper and lower reaches of the Yangtze River was also unfavorable. Furthermore, the observatory received a hurricane report yesterday, located at 11 degrees north latitude and 132 degrees east longitude, with the wind direction halted and wind force around 120 nautical miles, more than 2,000 nautical miles from Shanghai.

The National Diocesan Representatives Conference of the Chinese Catholic Progress Society held its fifth meeting yesterday. The lecture session began at 9:00 AM, with Zhao Wannan speaking on "The Mission of Catholic Youth," Fu Kaipeng on "The Cultivation of Catholic Youth," Xu Yunxi on "Catholic Youth and Prayer," Zhang Shiquan on "Catholic Youth and the Sodality of Our Lady," and Zhang Weiping on "Catholic Youth and the Army of the Eucharist." All the lectures focused on the knowledge, cultivation, and mission of Catholic youth in serving society. Following this, the plenary session on the Catholic Youth Movement was held, with Liu Hongxun reporting on the general situation of the work. Youth associations from Furen and Industry & Commerce schools also gave reports. After the reports, the discussion on Catholic youth issues began, led by Xiao Shiyi. Many resolutions were made regarding the expansion of the Catholic Youth Movement. Finally, Archbishop Cai gave a speech, stating that so-called religious children refer to the beginning stage of life under the age of fifteen. The Holy Church attaches great importance to the youth movement but pays even more attention to the children's movement. When Roman children were introduced to the Church, they were seen wearing Church badges on their chests. When asked what benefit they got from wearing these badges, the children replied that they wore these badges to protect the Holy Church, to protect the country and you (referring to the Pope). Hardoon Foreign Firm Encounters Rent Disputes 118

Many properties on Nanjing Road belong to the Hardoon Foreign Firm. Due to the economic downturn, tenants have been requesting rent reductions, leading to disputes. The letter jointly sent by Sanyi and others to the Hardoon Foreign Firm, and the letter from the Nanjing Road Citizens' First District Branch to various public organizations are recorded below: (1) The letter jointly sent by Sanyi Silk Shop and others to the Hardoon Foreign Firm stated, "We are writing to inform you that due to the economic downturn and poor business, we have jointly requested that your firm reduce the rent to promote prosperity and fairness. However, your firm adheres to its opinions or insists on the lease and refuses to compromise. We have no choice but to temporarily withhold rent payments and wait for your firm to reconsider. Unexpectedly, your firm has not taken the proper route to seek a solution and instead resorts to cunning or threats. Recently, your firm sent people to collect rent from our stores, gathering crowds to force payment, arbitrarily harassing us, and disrupting our business. This is beyond excessive and not a proper approach. We believe that your firm's oppressive actions will not only easily lead to conflicts between the two parties but also cause losses to our business. If any responsibility arises, we must ask your firm to bear it." (2) The letter to the Taxpaying Chinese Association stated, "(Details omitted). Our association, based on the requests of member stores on this road, has been working hard on the rent reduction movement and has repeatedly written to you for support. We are grateful for your agreement to support us. Since the beginning of the movement, it has been relatively smooth. Most landlords, both Chinese and foreign, are well aware of the difficulties faced by the stores and have agreed to reduce rents accordingly. However, the twenty or so tenants belonging to the Hardoon Foreign Firm have been peacefully requesting rent reductions based on the proportion of new rents charged to others. The foreign firm has been consistently evasive and has made insulting and unreasonable remarks. The tenants have had no choice but to temporarily suspend rent payments. Unexpectedly, the foreign firm not only refuses to reflect but also uses threats and oppression. In the past two days, they have sent seven or eight to more than ten strong men, along with shikari, to occupy the premises of Tongfu Silk Shop, Guanxin Hat Company, Dadong Socks Factory, and other stores, causing arbitrary harassment and making it impossible for these stores to operate. Yesterday afternoon around 3:00 PM, they sent more than ten people in several cars, as if facing a formidable enemy, to Sanyi Silk Shop, blocking the entrance, obstructing customers, occupying the tables, shouting abuse, causing the store to be in a state of chaos and unable to operate. Pedestrians on the road stopped to watch, causing traffic congestion and arousing public anger, almost leading to violence. The store had no choice but to close the iron gate, and the ten or so strong men left with a roar. All the stores on the road were furious upon hearing the news and anticipated that the foreign firm's oppressive tactics would be applied to each store one by one and would be endless. If not stopped, the consequences would be unimaginable. Therefore, they have requested assistance from our association. In addition to writing to the Public Works Department to order them to stop the oppressive acts and convening an emergency meeting to discuss countermeasures, we are writing to request that your association approve the transfer of a letter to the Public Works Department to protect the safety of taxpayers, protect businesses at all times, and stop the foreign firm's excessive actions to stabilize people's hearts and maintain the commercial market." The letters to the Citizens' General Assembly Rent Reduction Committee and various public organizations had similar content.

Water Cutoff Dispute Involving Fuyuan Lane on Kang Nai Tuo Road Leads to Lawsuit; Both Sides Have Reasons; Defendant Also Files Counterclaim 120

The houses in the Fuyuan Lane area on Kang Nai Tuo Road in West Shanghai are owned by Miao Shaoxian, a native of Yong, who is the issuing agent for the Hongda Lace Shop on Jingyuan Street, Mantingfang, Guangdong Road. Fuyuan Ji Property Management was established to rent the houses to Zhu Jinfu and others, with a monthly rent of 46 yuan per building, including water fees. Recently, Zhu and others, noting the poor economic conditions and slow business, as well as the high market prices and large expenses, jointly wrote to the landlord, requesting consideration of the business difficulties and a reduction in rent. They received a reply stating that if all tenants could pay off their back rent, the monthly rent would be reduced by 5 yuan and the water fee by 3 yuan. However, the water users would have to install their own water meters and pay directly. After calculating, Zhu and others concluded that this method was no different from not reducing the rent at all. They wrote back to the landlord, declaring the cancellation of the original agreement to reduce the rent and agreeing to pay the original rent. Unexpectedly, around 10:00 AM on the 15th of last month, the water supply in the area was suddenly cut off. Repeated negotiations were unsuccessful. Zhu and others, believing that the interruption of drinking water was a major threat to life, consulted lawyer Huang Xiubo, along with residents Chen Rongqing, Zhu Huirong, Yu Qingjiang, Lin Xinfu, and others, a total of fifteen households, and accused Miao Shaoxian of endangering public safety at the First Special District Court. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Wu Zehan of the Eighth Criminal Court summoned the defendant, Miao Shaoxian. Miao Shaoxian was unable to attend due to business in Yong, and lawyer Xi Yaoxi appeared in court to submit a defense and file a counterclaim, stating that because of the economic downturn, the original plaintiff, Miao Shaoxian, had voluntarily reduced the rent for the Fuyuan Lane houses under management. On June 23rd of this year, he sent separate letters to each counter-defendant, detailing the rent reduction plan and stating that due to high water fees, in order to safeguard the interests of both parties, starting from August 1st, in addition to voluntarily subsidizing each tenant with 3 yuan per month for water fees and paying the water meter deposit, the Shanghai Waterworks Company was instructed to install water meters for each household. He also instructed the tenants to pay the water meter deposit to the Shanghai Waterworks Company before July 21st. Unexpectedly, between August 12th and 16th, when the Shanghai Waterworks Company was updating its systems, the counter-defendants suddenly sent letters to the Fourth District Citizens' Association, requesting the restoration of the old system. The original plaintiff replied, explaining that the water meter deposit had already been paid, and all matters had been settled and could not be restored. Therefore, the water cutoff was actually due to the counter-defendants' failure to pay the water meter deposit on time, resulting in the cutoff by the Shanghai Waterworks Company, and the original plaintiff not only had no right to interfere but was now being accused of making false accusations. Judge Wu inquired and found that the original plaintiffs had mostly appointed representatives to the court today, and since the defendant had filed a counterclaim, the original plaintiffs were also counter-defendants and could not send representatives to the case. Therefore, he ordered that the case be rescheduled for hearing and that both parties must personally appear in court next time for questioning.

On the morning of the 4th of this month, detectives Wang Zhihao and Zhang Bingkun of the French Concession Police were patrolling the Jixiang Street area when they noticed a man named Sun Yuanqing acting suspiciously. Rickshaw drivers in the area south and west of Shanghai (i.e., the "Little Agreement") previously announced a strike on the morning of the 6th of last month in protest of the French Public Works Department's notice to register rickshaw drivers. Yang Cuiying (also known as Cao Yang), a local young woman, 21 years old, married Cao Xuewen two years ago through a matchmaker. She gave birth to a daughter last October. Recently, due to differences of opinion between husband and wife, Yang Cuiying returned to her mother's home and refused to return. The other day, Yang Cuiying hired lawyer Sun Biwu to file for divorce in the District Court. The complaint stated that three months after the marriage, the defendant's behavior changed. First, he claimed that the clinic he operated was losing money and pawned most of the plaintiff's dowry items. Then, he demanded that the plaintiff borrow money from others, and if she failed to do so, he would beat and scold her. The plaintiff initially thought that he was upset due to business problems, so she swallowed her anger and patiently offered kind words of advice. However, the defendant not only did not repent but became even more excessive, treating her as an enemy, and the marital relationship was severed. The plaintiff was disheartened and hopeless about the future, and requested a divorce, detailing five points: (1) request for divorce; (2) return of the plaintiff's wages of 330 yuan; (3) if the clothing and jewelry cannot be returned in their original condition, please return 1,230 yuan; (4) living expenses of 1,000 yuan; (5) the infant born should be raised by the plaintiff. He graduated from the Hongkou Obstetrics Hospital and moved to Niuzhuang, but the hospital was closed because he could not maintain it. He is now unemployed at home. He admitted that there were quarrels between husband and wife but denied any instances of beating. He disagreed with the divorce and requested to be reconciled, asking her to return home and live together. The judge, after obtaining the statements, repeatedly enlightened the plaintiff, stating that quarrels between husband and wife are common in families and should not be taken to extremes. He instructed both lawyers to mediate a settlement out of court. The case was adjourned for further hearing.

Publishing World 135

Illustrated Gazetteer of Six Great Buddhist Holy Sites in India Published. "The Buddhist Holy Sites in India" by Yishan Yun describes the places where Sakyamuni Buddha was born, attained enlightenment, and preached. During his eighty years of life, the Buddha spent about fifty years preaching and attaining enlightenment. He visited many places, but the six most important ones are: Bodh Gaya (place of enlightenment), Sarnath (Deer Park, the place of the first turning of the wheel of Dharma), Rajgir (the residence of the Vultures Peak), Shravasti (the location of the Jetavana Monastery), Kushinagar (the place of Nirvana), and Lumbini (the place of birth). Yishan Yun took photographs and provided brief descriptions, including detailed directions for pilgrims visiting these sites. It serves as a guide for those traveling to India to worship at Buddhist sites. Beautifully printed, priced at four jiao per copy. Published by the Buddhist Bookstore on Jiaozhou Road, Shanghai. Available at all branches in Shanghai and other cities.

Industrial and Commercial Management Monthly, Volume 2, Issue 9 Published. Scientific management is still in its infancy in our country, and there is a particular shortage of publications dedicated to this topic. Therefore, the China Industrial and Commercial Management Association, dedicated to promoting scientific management, publishes a monthly magazine for researchers. This issue (Volume 2, Issue 9) includes articles such as "The Evolution of Management and Its Fundamental Problems" by Tang Ze Yan, "Principles of Scientific Management" by Ju Zhe Yin, "Important Safety Issues" by Cheng Shou Zhong, "Production Management" by Zhu Xian Fang, and "Practical Ways to Promote Domestic Goods Overseas" by Shen Lin Yu. The articles are well-written and insightful. The annual subscription rate is two yuan, available at the Authors' Bookstore on Simalu (四马路).

This Year's "National Bank Yearbook" Published. The compilation and publication of bank yearbooks are considered urgent tasks in advanced countries around the world. The rise and fall of the banking industry in our country has spanned forty years, but statistical data is still lacking in concrete records, making it difficult to learn from the past and predict the future. Recognizing this, the Economic Research Office of the Bank of China began editing and publishing the "National Bank Yearbook" last summer, which has attracted attention from all sectors. The Economic Research Office of the Bank of China believes that the value of the yearbook lies in its continuous annual publication, allowing readers to understand the entire context. Therefore, the work of compiling and continuing the project has been undertaken, and the second "National Bank Yearbook" has now been published. The content materials of this edition are based on the changes of the past year and seek to be newer and more comprehensive. Superfluous information has been removed, and the essence has been retained to avoid unnecessary repetition. Bank annual reports, bank essays, indexes, and information on warehouses and godowns are all newly added this year. The operating reports of major banks over the years are particularly difficult for outsiders to collect, and even if they are collected, they are not necessarily complete. The index of bank essays is especially helpful for bankers and economists. These are the greatest advantages of this publication. The entire book consists of ten chapters and six appendices, totaling hundreds of thousands of words. The price is only eight yuan per copy, published by the Economic Research Office of the Bank of China at No. 50 Hankou Road, and sold by major bookstores throughout the country.

Chinese Medical Journal, Issue 111 Published. The Chinese Medical Journal, Issue 111, published by the Chinese Medical Association, was released yesterday. The main articles include: "Treatment and Prevention of Cholera" by Li Huansang of Guanghua Medical College in Guangzhou; "Alkaloids of Chinese Fangji" by Zhao Chengxia of the Institute of Materia Medica, Beiping Research Institute; "Research on the Chemical Composition of Asarum" by Zhao Chengxia and Zhu Renhong; "Pharmacological Research on Angelica sinensis" and "Research on Scutellaria baicalensis" by Li Shaoguang, Zhang Yaode, and Zhang Fachu of the Drug Research Laboratory of the Department of Health and Experimentation; "Report on Tuberculin Testing of 1091 People in Suzhou" by Chen Wangguan, Ji Sun Kuiyi of Suzhou Bo Xi Hospital; "Regional Anesthesia by Deeks" (Part 2), translated by Yang Ming of Nanjing Gulou Hospital; "Throat Swab Method in Diphtheria Diagnosis" and "Sodium and Adrenal Glands" translated by Dai Tianyou of the Department of Health; "Cardiovascular Syphilis"; and "The Recently Revised Articles of Association and Rules of Procedure of the Chinese Medical Association."

Weather Report 136

The weather forecast issued by the Xujiahui Observatory at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: Shandong and the surrounding areas, as well as the Yellow Sea, are partly cloudy and slightly cool with rain and strong northwest to north winds. The Yangtze River Basin is cloudy and cool with showers and strong northwest breezes due to a high-pressure system located in central China. The East China Sea has strong southerly to northeasterly winds. The small hurricane northwest of Palau is currently stationary and has not progressed. Its center was located within 120 miles of 11 degrees North latitude and 132 degrees East longitude at 1:00 PM. The wind force is unknown. Furthermore, the highest temperature in Shanghai within the 34 hours preceding 3:00 PM yesterday was 95.0 degrees, and the lowest was 77.5 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest temperature was 80.6 degrees, and the lowest was 70.7 degrees.

Unprecedented Spectacle: Domestic Cigarette Exhibition Opened at the Great World Yesterday; Nearly 100,000 Visitors from Noon to Evening 138

The Domestic Cigarette Exhibition, organized by the China Domestic Cigarette Maintenance Association, opened at the Great World (大世界) at 2:00 PM yesterday. Visitors received a box of Nanyang Tobacco Company's Red Golden Dragon or Airship brand cigarettes with their admission ticket. Starting today, Huacheng Tobacco Company will give away Golden Mouse brand cigarettes. The details of yesterday's events are as follows:

Opening Ceremony

The opening ceremony began at 2:00 PM, led by music. Key officials of the association, including Yuan Ludeng, Shen Weiting, Shen Xingde, Wang Junzhi, Ding Houqing, Jing Yimeng, Bao Gengsheng, Wu Linzhi, Sun Daosheng, Ding Zhenbo, Shen Xuewen, Zhang Xinliang, and Lu Shoulun, toured the exhibition grounds. The association's office also held an opening ceremony.

Exhibition Hall Arrangement

Starting yesterday, banners and slogans of the exhibition, as well as cigarette brand names of various tobacco companies, were hung all over the front of the Great World. A skillfully crafted archway was installed at the entrance. Inside the exhibition hall, a giant model of a domestic cigarette was specially made, towering high above the crowd. It was adorned with yellow paper lanterns and various small slogans. A large zoetrope (走马灯) was specially made on the fourth floor, creating a dazzling spectacle.

Novel Displays

Each participating factory had unique and different displays. Huacheng Today

Whether old or young, male or female, smokers all over the country know about Huacheng's Beauty and Golden Mouse brands. Today, Huacheng will give away a box of Golden Mouse brand cigarettes to each visitor with a Great World admission ticket.

Chess Competition

The Press and Domestic Cigarettes - One of the special supplements of the Chinese National Cigarette Maintenance Association Exhibition

Newspaper Opinion on National Cigarettes 139

The Chinese National Cigarette Maintenance Association held a National Cigarette Exhibition and published a special supplement. Thanks to the generosity and valuable advice of the gentlemen of the press, much encouragement was given to the cigarette factories and the people of the country. In particular, the cigarette factories received many methods and lessons on how to promote their products. Psychological Construction 140

— (Ma Yinliang)

I recently translated an article by Mr. Arnold, a commercial attaché at the American Consulate, who instructed us on how to develop foreign trade, and whose final conclusion was "Developing domestic trade is the foundation for developing foreign trade. To get foreigners to use Chinese goods, the Chinese people must first promote them themselves."

My friend Mr. Shen Junyi told us after returning from Europe about the situation in which the European people are happy to use domestic goods. The cigarettes smoked by the German people are not as good in form or flavor as foreign goods, but they smoke them with pleasure.

I believe that in the psychology of the people of the whole country, we should know that it is the duty of the Chinese people to use Chinese goods, and it is a shame to use foreign goods, unless it is when there is no domestic goods to replace them and they are indispensable. This kind of psychological construction of love for domestic goods can save China, now and in the future.

My opinion on the promotion of domestic goods is this. Now, in the midst of an enthusiastic wave of promoting domestic cigarettes, I think we should start with psychological construction first, so that there is great hope for the future of promoting domestic cigarettes.

What is Expected of the Press 141

Commemorating the 88th anniversary of the founding of the Republic of China, the gentlemen of the press each expressed their great opinions and published them in special publications. They each based their views on their individual personalities and positions to promote cigarettes. As the saying goes, "A single call from a high place will be echoed by all the mountains." This Association has nothing but deep gratitude and feels that it is unnecessary to disturb you with any further requests! However, I still have a few expectations, which I would like to express before my beloved gentlemen of the press; it is truly like family chatter, because of the depth of love, I do not realize the cost of offering words? If we can understand each other's hearts, then even if these extravagant hopes remain extravagant, it would be without regret for the press of our country!

It is said that the domestic cigarette industry has somewhat special circumstances compared to other domestic industries. This special circumstance is the essence of its special difficulties, and it is hoped that the press can strive to eliminate them. Let me briefly mention it.

People all say, "Cigarettes are a consumer good, how many people can afford it!" Or they say, "This is an exciting substance, which is harmful to public health!" Those who say this seem to forget that the money they spend can be used to buy an equivalent amount of pleasure; or that even a little excitement can be used to refresh, relieve worries, and cleanse the stomach. Only wine is unlimited, and can lead to chaos; if used extravagantly, even if the thing itself is very beneficial, it will eventually become a great harm! It is like purely entertaining novels and plays, which only contribute to regulating the mind and nourishing life. Should the world then place them in the ranks of art and popular education, or should they be criticized? However, cigarettes are used in the same way, and there is no need to criticize them. If we can establish a position and settle down, then our feelings will be balanced. Should the gentlemen of the press then disregard the words of others, uphold justice, and often spread the word, so as to correct the distorted consciousness of the masses?

The domestic cigarette industry has strong enemies abroad, and their power is obvious. Given our country's weakness, even dealing with them in the written word is met with much fear. At home, our compatriots have mixed attitudes, some are obsessed with foreign goods and cannot break free, while others are too lazy to think about it and are always in a state of indifference, thinking that cigarettes are a trivial matter and that it is not worth making a fuss about. Those in the cigarette industry are in a difficult position and are afraid to act rashly. Our gentlemen of the press should remember that you can see everything clearly, so please show the power of the host and the guest, clarify the distinction between benefits and harms, and point out clearly so that those with simple thoughts will not always be lost, and those with nervous minds will not be suspicious and mistaken? This Association is willing to follow behind the gentlemen of the press and shout, and will not hesitate to look back!

If the press has already given to this Association, and if it continues for a long time, then this help is beneficial to the national economy and the people's livelihood, and it is not only the blessing of the Cigarette Maintenance Association, but the blessing of the entire domestic cigarette industry!

How to Maintain Domestic Cigarettes 142

— (Wang Boqi)

I am a person who does not smoke cigarettes. Whenever I see people swallowing clouds and spitting fog from their mouths, I never know what kind of fun they have. However, no matter where or when, smokers can be seen everywhere, and it has become a common habit. The only thing it does is consume.

Originally, consumption should be reduced, so why must we maintain it? This is because society and people today have made smoking cigarettes an unbreakable habit in their lives, and there is absolutely no possibility of quitting. In fact, it has changed from consumption to a need. In that case, instead of smoking foreign cigarettes, it is better to think about it from a negative point of view and promote domestic goods and maintain domestic cigarettes, which can also reduce the outflow of more than 10 million yuan every year, maintain the workers of many cigarette factories, and the farmers in the tobacco-producing areas, and also increase the large income of the national treasury. The establishment of the China Domestic Cigarette Maintenance Association is to awaken the psychology of the people to love domestic goods. It has a great significance and is worthy of admiration. However, how can domestic cigarettes be maintained? According to the contribution of this layman, the people should, of course, fulfill their national responsibilities and must smoke domestic cigarettes. On the part of the cigarette merchants, they should also work hard to improve and strive for excellence in their products. The price should be commensurate with the value, and they should unite with their peers and encourage each other in order to be successful. I sincerely advocate this and look forward to the efforts of the members of the Maintenance Association.

Three Battle Lines 143

— (Mi Li Fang)

Although cigarettes are a kind of consumable, they are indispensable for intellectuals, especially writers. Originally, China did not have cigarettes. After they flowed in from foreign countries, people generally found them convenient and slowly all started smoking them. From then on, the floodgates opened wide, and a large amount of money flowed into foreign cities every year, an uncountable sum. Seeing such a crisis, domestic cigarette factories were established one after another.

In fact, it is a matter of course for Chinese people to use Chinese goods, and it is also natural for Chinese people to smoke Chinese cigarettes. There is no need to explain it further. Now, to wait for domestic cigarette merchants to promote, advocate, and persuade Chinese people to smoke Chinese cigarettes is already an extremely painful thing for the domestic factories themselves. And the mentality of Chinese people not valuing domestic goods can also be seen from this.

Therefore, to promote and maintain domestic cigarettes, it can be discussed in the following three aspects:

(1) Reforming the psychology of Chinese people. Generally, those who smoke foreign cigarettes do so out of a mentality of worshiping foreign goods and considering themselves wealthy. Therefore, this kind of mentality and habit should be broken first. In fact, among the current domestic cigarettes, there are also very high-quality products that are sufficient to match foreign cigarettes. Recently, I saw that a foreign-style grand hotel has also started selling domestic cigarettes, which shows that the psychology of Chinese people is gradually changing, which is also a gratifying thing.

(2) Improving the quality of domestic products themselves. Domestic cigarettes often become popular when they are first produced, but then gradually decline. The quality also slowly becomes inferior to the initial products. The taste of the cigarettes cannot be maintained at this standard. Therefore, domestic cigarette merchants, in order to have Chinese people smoke domestic cigarettes, should do their best to improve and progress in terms of technical and capital possibilities.

(3) Promoting domestic goods through publicity. Publicity is of course also the most important task. Small shops that sell cigarettes should be made aware of the importance of smoking domestic cigarettes and understand that they should do their best to promote domestic cigarettes. For the intellectual community, there should be constant promotional materials to stimulate them, such as pamphlets. Finally, it is hoped that the government authorities, within the possible range of financial resources, will give domestic cigarette merchants a reduction in taxes. There are many ways to promote, and this is only one of the important ones.

Two Purposes 144

— (Wang Jilu)

Although cigarettes are not food, they now occupy a place among commodities and are becoming increasingly popular. People need them as much as they need rice and wheat. China initially did not have cigarettes. Since their introduction from Europe and the West, everyone has had one in their hand, and they have become popular throughout the country. Statistics show that the amount of money exported each year due to cigarette smoking is immeasurable. People with ambition have therefore started their own domestic cigarette factories to resist foreign goods. Although there are dozens of domestic cigarette factories, they produce thousands of varieties of cigarettes. However, due to domestic and foreign troubles in recent years, the country is in turmoil, rural areas are bankrupt, industry and commerce have failed, and finance is extremely tight as a result. Livelihoods are difficult. Therefore, the cigarette industry has also shown signs of decline. Leaders in the cigarette industry have therefore established the China National Goods Cigarette Maintenance Association, hoping to seek the revival of domestic cigarettes. This is truly a good strategy. In this critical period for domestic cigarettes, what methods should we use to revive and rise up? People have long called for "National Goods to Save the Country." Smoking domestic cigarettes means using domestic goods. Using domestic goods is the first step towards achieving the meaning of National Goods to Save the Country. Therefore, "National Goods to Save the Country" can also be called "Cigarettes to Save the Country." In the current period, we should start by saving the cigarette industry, and then we can save the country and the people. To revive domestic cigarettes, there are two purposes. One is the cigarette factory, and the other is the smoker. Cigarette factories should strive for excellence in their products and adhere to the principle of small profits. Companies in the same industry should have a spirit of competition, but they should also have a sincere heart of mutual love and protection. Do not shed blood because of commercial warfare, and do not slander each other out of jealousy. Then the future will be bright, and reviving from decline will be just around the corner. As for smokers, everyone should have a cigarette in their hand, and domestic products should be valued. While we should not have xenophobic thoughts, we cannot be without a patriotic heart. Break the vanity of worshiping foreign cigarettes and eliminate the bad habit of despising domestic cigarettes. Introduce them to everyone and do your best to promote them. Smoking to save the country is a win-win situation. Strive, cigarette factories! Work hard, smokers!

Correcting "Foreign Obsession" 145

— (Chen Yaozhu)

I believe that the decline of China's cigarette industry has many causes, but the Chinese people's psychology of worshiping foreign goods is a major blow. Looking at middle-class and above families in our country, the cigarettes they smoke are mostly imported goods, as if they are not enough to show their high status. If this kind of psychology is not eliminated one day, domestic cigarettes will be hindered one day. Therefore, to seek the revival of domestic cigarettes, we must first correct the Chinese people's psychology of "foreign obsession" and make everyone feel honored to smoke domestic cigarettes and ashamed to buy foreign cigarettes. Then domestic cigarettes will have hope of revival.

As for the domestic cigarette industry itself, at this time of extreme business decline, it is especially important to redouble its efforts. The products must be excellent, and the costs must be reduced to meet the needs of the Chinese people. Although it is said that the Chinese people's psychology of worshiping foreign goods is too deep, if there are exquisite domestic goods, it is enough to change their usual perception. Is it not true of the towels we use every day? Twenty years ago, those sold in our country were all iron anchor brand from a certain country. Since the advent of the domestic triangle brand towels, the Chinese people have been happy to buy and use them because of their excellent quality and low price. The iron anchor brand then disappeared from our country. The heart of patriotism, everyone has it. If one abandons cheap and good domestic goods and does not use them, and would rather buy inferior foreign goods at a high price, unless one is insane, how could one do this? Therefore, I hope that the domestic cigarette industry will broaden its horizons, carefully study its products, and take the cause as a prerequisite, rather than be greedy for immediate profits and commit suicide. Regarding the same industry, we should also, as the Maintenance Association declared, unite with each other and consolidate the united front. It is not appropriate to seek one's own interests and be profit-seeking, giving others an opportunity to take advantage of, and causing a crisis of being defeated individually. If we proceed in this way and move forward, the revival of domestic cigarettes can be expected.

After the Visit: Additional Thoughts 146

— (Zhen Chao)

The news community is deeply enthusiastic about promoting domestic cigarettes. This time, we visited the managers of various newspapers and received a very warm reception, with valuable opinions expressed. Among these many proposals that contribute to domestic cigarettes, let us make a small summary.

Taken together, these can be divided into the following three main arguments: (1) We should ask the Chinese people to first reform their psychology and cultivate the habit of loving and using domestic goods; (2) Domestic cigarette manufacturers should do their best to improve and upgrade their goods within the possible range of technology and economics; (3) In terms of promotion, we should make promoters do their best to promote domestic cigarettes.

These are almost unanimous arguments. We sincerely hope that the Chinese people and domestic cigarette manufacturers will encourage each other.

Wishing a Victorious Future 147

— (Wang Loubing)

When writers conceive ideas, they often hold a cigarette in their hand, inhaling and exhaling, which is enough to add to the elegant mood. However, most of these consumer goods are imported from abroad or manufactured in factories set up in China with foreign investment. Therefore, the market is filled with foreign goods. The amount of cash flowing out of the country every year is huge. If this continues without seeking relief, how can the people bear it, how can the country bear it? Gentlemen, to maintain domestic cigarettes is also a deep-hearted wish. Therefore, I am very happy to see the success of the gentlemen. I will speak slowly and wish you a smooth future.

Sports News

Opening of the Jiangsu Provincial Games, Opening Ceremony, Speeches by Zhou Fo Hai, etc. Heroes of Both Sexes Fight in a Great Wind and Rain 148

(Special Dispatch from Zhenjiang) The opening of the Fourth Jiangsu Provincial Games was held at 8 a.m. on the 12th at the Provincial Stadium. More than a thousand representatives from various agencies and guests attended. Chen Guofu, the president of the General Assembly, was unable to return to the province to participate due to matters in Beijing. After the meeting, all the athletes toured the venue for a week. Zhou Fohai delivered the opening speech, followed by speeches by Yu Jingtao and Zhang Gongren. The details are recorded below:

Speech by President Zhou

In brief, he said, everyone, the Fourth Jiangsu Provincial Games opened today. At this opening, there are nine things I want to report to you and hope you will pay attention to. First, the reason why we decided to open today is that the weather is cool at this time, and the spirit of the athletes can be invigorated and enterprising. Who knows that the weather these days is still very hot, which is a deficiency in this conference. However, you have the spirit of hard work, healthy bodies, and strong wills. You will definitely be able to endure hardship. In the future, when we fight for our nation, the labor will be even more severe than it is now. So take this opportunity to exercise our physique. However, in this hot weather, everyone must pay special attention to diet and clothing to prevent the occurrence of diseases. This is the first point I hope everyone will pay attention to. Second, everyone should know the spirit and meaning of the Games. The meaning of the Games is not only in the technical competition, but most importantly, it is a training in social morality. How can our society progress? Because after competition, there must be victory or defeat. The winner exists, and the loser is eliminated. Everyone works hard to compete for survival, and society will naturally progress. There is also a saying that society cannot compete, and the progress of society is in mutual assistance and cooperation, because competition is tantamount to killing each other. When the two sides compete, each other's strengths are offset. The most obvious example is international war. In times of war, I do not know how many lives, forces and spirits must be sacrificed. It can gradually degrade society. Therefore, it is believed that mutual assistance and cooperation can make society progress, but we believe that the progress of society requires war, but competition must be based on proper methods. The so-called proper methods, the first is fair conditions, the second is public mode, and the second is a fair attitude. Competition under these three circumstances can promote social progress. The Games are a representative of legitimate competition. When we watch the race, everyone's starting point is the same. For example, in the competition, the number of people on both sides is equal, which is a fair condition. Everyone should perform their skills under fair conditions. When the game is in progress, there are many referees and spectators watching, and there is no opportunity to speculate and take advantage of the opportunity. This is completely an open way. Third, the attitude should be fair. The so-called fair attitude is that there are many rules during the game, and everyone must abide by those rules. If any of the athletes violate the rules, the conference will stop their attendance. Therefore, the Games can represent legitimate competition. If we promote this kind of legitimate competition to society, it will definitely make society progress. Therefore, the Games are also a driving force for social progress. This is the true meaning of the Games. Finally, what needs to be known is that since there is competition, there will certainly be victory and defeat, but we take victory and defeat too seriously, and often break the rules in our eagerness to win, and take actions outside the rules, which loses the meaning of the Games. Therefore, we do not want to win by breaking the rules, otherwise this kind of victory is a disgrace. We must seek victory in fair competition to be glorious. I hope that everyone will not pay too much attention to victory or defeat, but must pay attention to the spirit of the conference. The above three points are reported to everyone at today's opening, and I hope you will pay more attention.

Afterwards, Committee Member Zhang, representing the Provincial Party Department, and Director Yu, representing Chairman Chen, delivered speeches one after another.

Gu Jingchu crossed the Chencang River secretly, as if entering an uninhabited place. The goalkeeper of District 2 was isolated and helpless, and was pulled back by one, and the situation became tense again. International Swimming Competition in a Storm: Held at the City Swimming Pool Last Night; Jian Erjie Overwhelms Weilzi in 100m Breaststroke 160

The grand international swimming performance, organized by Sheng Da Zhuang, was held at the City Swimming Pool in the city center at 9 o'clock last night. More than a thousand people, including Mayor Wu, Li Dachao, and guests from all walks of life, attended. The various programs were extremely exciting and broke all the city records. The results were wonderful. Finally, Mayor Wu hosted a banquet for all the athletes, and the event ended in great joy around 11 o'clock. It is a pity that the wind was strong and cold. A reporter from the Guojue News Agency investigated and recorded the details as follows:

Weather Update

Last night, all the lighting equipment in the city's new pool was fully configured. Electric lights surrounded the stands like long snakes, and the wall lamps everywhere were also brightly lit. Especially the radiating lights in the pool were the most beautiful. Being in it was like being in a crystal palace. Although there was a heavy downpour last night, there were still more than a thousand spectators. At 8 o'clock sharp, the competition began. The City Police Department band played music on the field, and after each competition, Mr. Shen Siliang announced the results in Chinese and English via wireless radio.

Competition Situation

After the competition started, the first event was the 50-meter freestyle. Liang Huisheng from our country competed fiercely with Boton. As a result, he ranked second with a difference of one meter, but he had already overwhelmed Pan Qiyou, the champion of the previous Hong Kong, by half a meter. No one from our country originally joined the 200-meter freestyle. Shi Bogen played the role temporarily. As a result, Shi Bogen fell behind Pan Morda by more than 20 meters. One of the most exciting events was the 100-meter breaststroke. Jian Erjie took the lead all the way after starting, reaching 35 meters away. Even Wang Weilzi ranked second. Jian Erlian won the third place, which is also commendable. In the 100-meter freestyle, Liang Huisheng, with his long-term illness, was not ashamed to lose to Haimeng. Hai's results broke the national record. Our country did not participate in the 100-meter backstroke and women's 50-meter. The 300-meter relay was temporarily changed to 200 meters.

Mayor's Banquet

After the competition, Mayor Wu Tiecheng hosted a banquet on the first floor of the new pool for all the Chinese and Western athletes from the city who participated in the Hong Kong-Shanghai swimming competition. Secretary-General Yu Hongjun, Section Chief Li Dachao, and Shen Siliang, Executive Director of the National Sports Association, accompanied him. During the banquet, the mayor gave a speech, saying, "I am very pleased that the grand international competition tonight has been graced by the presence of Chinese and Western athletes. I hope that this new pool can be used more in the future to improve our country's swimming technology. In this Hong Kong-Shanghai swimming competition, Shi and Jian were selected for the first time, which is a glorious page in the history of swimming in our city. Tonight, I, in the name of the mayor, have prepared a silver cup to be presented to the city's inter-city representative team, and I hope that this trip to Hong Kong can bring victory," etc. Mr. Hekesilai, Chairman of the City Amateur Swimming Association, received the mayor's large silver cup and handed it over to Haimeng, the captain of the inter-city team. They took a group photo together and dispersed in great joy around 11 o'clock. All ten members of the inter-city team will board the President Cleveland at the New Customs Wharf at 11 o'clock tonight and set sail for Hong Kong at 5 o'clock tomorrow morning, led by Hekesilai.

City Private School Teacher Training Class: Hired Lecturers to Give Lectures; Gu Yinqian and Others Hired as Lecturers; Scheduled to be Held Once Every Saturday 166

The private school teacher training class organized by the City Education Bureau was previously designated in six schools in the district, including the Municipal Agricultural Field, Caotang, Tanzhen, Caonan, Yucai, and Jingcun. It opened on September 1st, and the Education Bureau appointed Ling Xianwen, Tang Jingxiu, Gao Jie, Lü Xinfu, Shen E, and Sun Shiju to participate. According to the reports of these members, the number of private school teachers in Caotang is too small, with only twelve actually attending. The number of people in Tanzhen and Yucai schools is too large, reaching more than 80 people, which is impossible to arrange. After receiving the report, the Education Bureau believes that the number of people in Caotang is too small, does not meet the regulations, and is not economical, so it should be stopped immediately, and all private school teachers should be merged into the agricultural field for management. The number of people in Yucai and Tanzhen schools is too large, making teaching difficult, so they should be divided into classes for teaching. The school has been informed to comply. In addition to the required courses such as civic training, Mandarin, arithmetic, common sense, single-level primary school teaching methods, and knowledge that private school teachers must know, there are also special lectures for all subjects in the training class, which are held once every Saturday evening. The teachers for the special lectures have been separately appointed by the Education Bureau. All the hired lecturers are municipal primary school principals with rich teaching experience and in-depth research, as well as inspectors from the Education Bureau. The list of special lecturers and lecture topics is copied as follows: Gu Yinqian, discussion of practical education problems; Qian Xuanqing, primary school teaching materials; Tong Shicha, private school administration; Chai Zifei, social problems; Xu Shushen, political research guidance; Wang Jingqing, health education; Wang Jianren, implementation of training; Gao Jie, child psychology; Qian Songping, principles of education; Lü Xinfu, practical problems in private school reform. The above ten people will give a lecture once a week, and five weeks can be lectured in five places, which can be completed in ten weeks.

Training Directors and Civic Teachers: Those Who Do Not Report Their Work Will Be Sanctioned 167

The Central People's Movement Guidance Committee stipulates that all training directors and civic teachers who have passed the examination and have been hired by various schools should report their work progress each semester to the Examination Committee for review. The Committee for Reviewing the Qualifications of Training Directors and Civic Teachers in Secondary Schools in this city has long issued an order to comply with it. According to Yu Zhongju, a member of the committee, the reporter of the National News Agency said yesterday that many training directors and civic teachers from various schools have submitted their work situation in the last semester, but there are still many who have not reported it. It is now planned to impose sanctions on the training directors and civic teachers of various schools who have not fulfilled the reporting procedures, according to the central regulations.

Little Boy (4) (4) 169

— Original by American writer Louisa May Alcott, translated by Zheng Xiaocang (Zonghai)

The sincerity expressed in his words and expression made Mrs. Shu unconsciously put her hand on his shoulder, and said to him in her most affectionate tone:

"Then come with your friend, Ned; I think we must find a way for him, without you having to give up your position."

Ned ran off happily and soon returned, followed by the most lackluster big boy, who slunk in with his eyebrows drooped, looked around, half fierce and half resentful on his face, which made Mrs. Pei whisper to herself:

"A piece of bad goods, I'm afraid."

"This is Don," Ned introduced him, thinking he would be welcomed.

"Ned tells me you're willing to come and join us," Mrs. Shu began in a kindly voice.

But only a rough, abrupt, simple answer came—"Yes."

"Don't you have any friends to take care of you?"

"No."

"Say 'No, ma'am,'" Ned gently told him.

"Who cares!" Don answered resentfully.

"How old are you?"

"About fourteen."

"You look more than that. What can you do?"

"I can do almost anything."

"If you stay, we want you to be like everyone else, besides playing, you also have to work and learn. Are you willing to agree to that condition?"

"Doesn't matter to give it a try."
